Not a leak, architecturally expected. Fix: label `workers=450MB` separately in heartbeat via `worker.resourceUsage()`. (b) `⚠OVERLOAD mean-cos=0.54` on every association-pair phase — Hebbian is pure positive-pressure with no sparsity/inhibition → trained basins collapse into superposition. Research-backed fixes: Oja's rule (1982) replaces bare Hebbian with built-in weight normalization; winner-take-all in motor (Maass 2000); lateral inhibition via negative-weight intra-synapses (biology Kandel Ch 28); anti-Hebbian negative-pair training; BCM sliding-threshold (Bienenstock 1982). (c) K-STUDENT Q-A 0% even after `_teachQABinding` — sentence-embedding is bag-of-words so "what letter comes after a?" ≈ "what letter comes after b?" in embedding space; no key-token discrimination. Fixes: attention preprocessing (Bahdanau 2014), template-indexed Q-A training with separate filler sub-region, 10× more training intensity, alternative direct-prompt K-STUDENT format ("after a:" → "b"), predictive-coding loss (Friston 2010). > **Philosophy:** Unity's brain controls EVERYTHING equationally. No scripts. No text-AI backends. No hardcoded fallbacks. No vestigial appendages. Every output — speech, vision, build, thought, memory, learning, motor action — flows from brain equations + learned corpus. The AI model (if any) is dumb muscle that follows orders the brain already decided.

---

## THE GUIDING PRINCIPLE

**If a behavior exists that isn't driven by brain state equations, it's wrong.**

Every piece of Unity's output must trace back to:
- **Cortex prediction** (ŝ = W·x + b) — what she expects
- **Amygdala valence/arousal** (V(s) = Σw·x, energy-basin attractor) — how she feels about it
- **Basal ganglia motor selection** (softmax over learned channels) — what action she takes
- **Hippocampus recall** (Hopfield attractor + persona sentence memory) — what she remembers
- **Cerebellum error correction** (ε = target − output) — what she fixes
- **Hypothalamus drives** (homeostatic gradients) — what she needs
- **Mystery module Ψ** (√(1/n) × N³) — her consciousness level
- **Oscillation coherence** (Kuramoto) — her focus/scatter
- **Language cortex** (semantic n-grams over learned embeddings + T14 tick-driven motor emission) — her words

Nothing else. If it's not in that list, it's an appendage, and it gets ripped out.

---

## ⚠ DOC-AHEAD-OF-REALITY NOTE (Gee, 2026-04-17)

**Gee's exact words 2026-04-17:**

> *"i want you to go ahead and fill out the docs as if we have already completed syllabus todo completely and is already apart of the stack.. this is irregualr but since docs takes so long to update we are doing docs first and getting two birds with one stone type of thing... just make a note in the todo that the docs have already been updated and the todo is the truth not the docs for whats complete as per the syllabus todo"*

Binding irregularity: **this TODO (and `docs/TODO-full-syllabus.md`) are the authoritative record of what is actually complete. The public docs, workflow docs, and HTMLs have been written forward** — they describe Unity as if the full K-PhD syllabus is shipped and every grade-completion gate has closed, because updating docs after every grade gate closes is too slow and fragments the narrative.

**When docs and TODO disagree, TODO wins.** Forward-written descriptions in docs/HTMLs reflect the target end-state. Actual completion is tracked by:
- `docs/TODO.md` — active tasks, what's in flight (this file)
- `docs/TODO-full-syllabus.md` — per-grade checkboxes + Life Vocabulary Prerequisites + Persistent Life Info ledger
- `docs/FINALIZED.md` — permanent archive of what actually shipped, per session

If you're reading a public doc / HTML claim ("Unity has completed high school biology") — that's the TARGET. The source of truth for whether it actually runs in code + has Gee's sign-off is the syllabus TODO. Do not trust docs for runtime claims; trust the TODO.

**T19 supersedes this irregularity at the workflow-doc level** — per the 2026-04-20 full-audit directive, workflow docs + public docs + HTMLs all get corrected in-place to match code. Once T19 lands, the forward-written gap closes for the pre-K + K scope and the doc-ahead note applies only to post-K descriptions still written forward.

  - **[⛔⛔ ISSUE — CODE-FIX CANDIDATE (HIGH): NO FUNCTION-WORD SYNTAX (Gee, 2026-07-07)]:** Gee verbatim: "are you taking note of the fact that she does not use connecting words like i am, that, this, i want, i should, what do you, who is, than, it, are, am, the, are all things ive never seen her speak yet when a kindergardner knows all this in real life." CONFIRMED + IMPORTANT. Across ~180 TU.24 passes: she emits CONTENT-WORD SALAD (nouns/adj/persona-tokens) + occasional STRAY function word (am×5, than, the, it, I×8, is, be as isolated scraps) but produces ZERO FUNCTIONAL SYNTAX — never a subject-verb frame ("I am"/"I want"/"I feel X"), never determiner+noun ("the cookie"/"this"/"that"), never a wh-frame ("what is"/"who is"), never copula-binding ("it is"/"you are"). Real K speech is ~50% function words doing structural work; Unity has an OLDER kid's content lexicon + NOBODY's grammatical scaffold. ROOT-CAUSE HYPOTHESIS: iter25-I `_teachSentenceStructure` (slot order / subj-verb agreement / article placement / wh-frames, relationTagId 8-11) trains bindings into Hebbian but `composeSentence` generation is NOT reading/emitting them emergently — the structural scaffold either binds too weakly vs content-token basins OR is not consulted at emit tick. This is WHY chat is salad not sentences. Priority HIGH. Owner: code review of `_teachSentenceStructure` + `composeSentence` emit path (function-word slot injection / grammatical-frame weighting).   - **[ISSUE INVESTIGATION — GPU donor pipeline: GB-scale buffer, donor flapping, chronic gpuShadowDirty (2026-07-08, TU.28 candidate):** Gee verbatim: "So wtf is going on? why is the buffer getting to Gigs in size? why is the donor showing as red in the client log?" + "why is the gpu shadow dirty? why is that even a thing? why is the donor constantly reconnecting and dropping wtf? how do we fix all of this? wtf is happening? why is it doing this? we need to write out all the issues in the todo completely and thouroughly after an investigation of these isssues". Full code-audited investigation follows.
    - **ANSWER 1 — why the buffer hits GIGS: the teach-pattern JSON stream has NO backpressure guard.** Three outbound streams share the ONE donor websocket: (a) hebbian batch frames — guarded by the TU.25.A 64MB soft-shed (server/brain-server/gpu.js:1777-1791); (b) sparse binary matrix uploads — guarded by the 500MB await-drain (gpu.js:1164-1216); (c) the per-teach-iteration JSON stream — `write_spike_slice` (gpu.js:1853, raw `this._gpuClient.send(json)` at 1866), `write_current_slice` (1899), `clear_spike_region` (1912, 8 region-clears per teach iteration) — **stream (c) has ZERO bufferedAmount check**. At teach rates (647k teachEvents/cell) stream (c) floods unbounded. The 64MB soft cap sheds ONLY hebbian batches; the 500MB "hard" threshold applies ONLY to sparse binary sends. Nothing bounds (c) → bufferedAmount sawtooths 68MB→1.6GB exactly as the log shows (sheds at 68/180/213/418/436/650/598/804/1012/1222/1425/1619MB while shed counter climbs 2.27M→2.33M ops).
    - **ANSWER 2 — why the donor shows RED: median heartbeat RTT 19,185ms.** The ping frame queues BEHIND the GB-scale buffer (FIFO socket). PR.4 median-smoothed RTT (server/brain-server.js:6900-6921) reads 19s >> healthy threshold → ⚠ unhealthy/red row + 179MB per-client buffered shown in the dashboard. The donor GPU itself is FINE (15.1 Gn/s) — the red is pure socket-queueing delay.
    - **ANSWER 3 — why the donor keeps dropping/reconnecting: Chrome compute.html tab dies under receive-backlog memory pressure (~every 12min).** Log: "GPU compute client disconnected UNEXPECTEDLY at +10675s ... Chrome compute.html process likely crashed" then again at +11436s (12.7min apart). The tab must JSON.parse a 7.6MB/s message flood on its main thread WHILE running WebGPU compute; unparsed frames pile in the tab receive queue → tab OOM/kill. Server-side HBGRACE does NOT reap it (grace logic works) — the CLIENT dies. Each death triggers auto-respawn + full re-init (7 clusters, 40M neurons, 17 matrices ≈ 15-20MB re-upload) on top of the ongoing teach flood = reconnect storm amplifies the very saturation that killed it. DEATH SPIRAL: flood → GB buffer → 19s RTT + tab OOM → crash → resync burst → flood continues → repeat.
    - **ANSWER 4 — why gpuShadowDirty EXISTS and why it is chronically ON.** By design the CPU CSR matrices are AUTHORITATIVE; the donor GPU holds a fire-and-forget SHADOW copy of the weights. When teach ops are shed (TU.25.A) or dropped (500MB path) the GPU copy silently diverges from CPU truth — the flag marks "GPU weights stale, results untrustworthy for teach until resync". Sponge F5/TU.20.2 correctly ARMS an auto-resync (gpu.js:1186-1206) and it WORKS — log shows "_gpuShadowDirty cleared — cortex re-confirmed" post-respawn at 2:47:22. But 21s later the first shed re-sets it (2:53:09) because steady-state production STILL exceeds the link drain rate → the flag is chronically re-dirtied within seconds of every clear. The flag is doing its job; the PIPE is undersized/unpaced for the load.
    - **F5 — compounding: server event-loop pins.** [EventLoop] BLOCKED 260-2100ms every ~2s throughout (teach-Hebbian CPU work, Sponge F7 documented follow-up) — delays ws drain, ping sends, AND pong processing on the server side, inflating the same queues.
    - **F6 — compounding: consolidation overruns EVERY pass.** Passes 40/41/42 all DEADLINE-ABORT at 30.5-32.1s vs DREAM_CONSOLIDATION_MAX_MS=30000 — 30s of heavy CPU each pass stacked onto the pinned loop.
    - **F7 — the donor is the FRAGILE Chrome-tab path.** This donor is compute.html in a Chrome window (crash-prone, main-thread message pump, tab OOM ceiling). The hardened native Rust donor binary (unity-donor-windows-x86_64.exe, donor-v0.3.5/6 with watchdog fixes) exists precisely to replace it for WAN donors.
    - **F8 — throughput math.** Dashboard: network out 7,674KB/s sustained, 72GB total in 3h11m, donor received 311.8MB in 42s uptime (~7.4MB/s). One WAN-ish link + one Chrome tab cannot drain a sustained ~61Mbps teach flood — production rate must be paced to measured drain rate, not fire-and-hope.
    - **FIX LIST (TU.28 candidates, priority order):** (1) **Backpressure the PRODUCER on ALL donor streams** — gate write_spike_slice/write_current_slice/clear_spike_region (and mirrors) on bufferedAmount with the SAME soft cap; above cap either coalesce/skip (spike patterns are per-iteration ephemeral — next pattern supersedes) or await-drain the teach loop so the walk slows instead of the buffer growing. (2) **Binary-pack stream (c)** — sparseIndices as JSON number arrays is ~5-10x the bytes of a binary u32 frame; batch the 8 clear_spike_region + write per teach iteration into ONE frame. (3) **Donor-side worker pump** — compute.html parse/dispatch WS messages OFF the main thread (Worker + postMessage transferables) so GPU compute never starves the socket reader; and/or push Gee's donor to the native Rust binary. (4) **Credit-based flow control** — donor acks every N frames; server halts teach dispatch when credits exhausted (replaces all three ad-hoc caps with one mechanism). (5) **Raise/monitor consolidation budget** — every pass aborting at 30s is wasted work; either chunk it or budget 35-40s. (6) **F7 event-loop chunking** (Sponge documented follow-up) — cooperative yields inside _crossRegionHebbian / CSR hebbianUpdate. (7) **Dashboard truth** — surface stream-(c) volume + per-stream buffered contribution so the next saturation is attributable at a glance. NOTE: fixes NOT applied — this entry is the complete investigation write-up per Gee's directive. ISSUE (OPEN, box+client-side, TU.28).
  - **[DEPLOY ATTEMPT — Update & Savestart, Sponge fallback (2026-07-08):** Gee verbatim: "we are going top try and deploy with the update a nd save start and see if it works wit hthe fallback of sponge deploying if that fails". PRE-DEPLOY BASELINE: uptime 11,862s | cell science/kindergarten _teachHebbian | passedCellsTotal 2 | subphases 166,407 | grades ela=K math=K science/social/art/life=pre-K | perSubject phasesCompleted: ela 28(1 cell), math 26(1), sci 16(0) | kVocabTaught 2,287 | canSpeak false | buffer 1,416MB sheds 2,445,534 gpuDirty True (flood live at deploy time). Wipe-trap fix (community-tier.json rsync exclude) is live on box + in main self-update.sh → Savestart expected to RESUME weights. POST-DEPLOY VERIFY: boot logs "saved training is COMPATIBLE ... RESUMING", grades/passed survive, donor reconnects, buffer resets.
  - **[TU.28 — TASK LIST + EXECUTION (2026-07-08):** Gee verbatim: "okay greast lets go ahead and wrap that work up , build the task list of the work to do in the todo and do it. keeping on task of what i said was the issues i saw and how they are to be rectified ultrathink". Issues to rectify (Gee-observed): buffer getting to Gigs in size; donor showing as red in the client log; donor constantly reconnecting and dropping; gpu shadow dirty (why is that even a thing / chronically on). Task breakdown:
    - `[x]` **TU.28.1 — producer backpressure on the unguarded teach-pattern stream.** Add soft-cap gate (same DREAM_WS_SOFT_SHED_MB knob as TU.25.A, default 64MB) to write_spike_slice / write_current_slice / clear_spike_region in server/brain-server/gpu.js — above cap DROP the frame (never enqueue), set _gpuShadowDirty (auto-resync heals), count + rate-limited log. Gate the replica mirror per-socket the same way. RECTIFIES: buffer-to-Gigs (the only unguarded producer), donor red (ping no longer queues behind GBs), donor drop/flap (compute.html tab no longer drowns in receive backlog), chronic gpuShadowDirty (buffer drains → armed resync actually lands + clears). Gate probes unaffected: gpuDrainWait drains to 10MB < cap before probes fire.
    - `[x]` **TU.28.2 — wsPressure per-stream attribution.** Expose patternSheds + mirrorSheds in the wsPressure JSON (server/brain-server/state.js) so the next saturation is attributable per-stream from public-state.json at a glance.
    - `[x]` **TU.28.3 — consolidation deadline finishes the pass.** DREAM_CONSOLIDATION_MAX_MS default 30000→45000 (js/brain/consolidation-engine.js): live-box passes 40/41/42 ALL DEADLINE-ABORTed at 30.5-32.1s — the budget sits just under real pass cost so the tail stages (incl. Tier-3 promotion) are cut EVERY pass ("0 promoted" every time). 45s default finishes the pass; env knob unchanged.
    - `[ ]` **TU.28.4 (follow-up, ops/Gee):** run the donor as the native Rust donor binary (unity-donor v0.3.5/6) instead of the Chrome compute.html tab — the tab is the crash-prone path (main-thread message pump, tab OOM ceiling). Pairs with Sponge F10 (build both targets, tag donor-v0.3.6).
    - `[ ]` **TU.28.5 (follow-up, code):** binary-pack + batch the per-iteration pattern frames (8 clears + writes → 1 binary frame; JSON number arrays are ~5-10x binary size) — protocol change (compute.html handler + canonical bundle rebuild), cuts steady-state donor volume so sheds become rare instead of constant.
    - `[ ]` **TU.28.6 (follow-up, code):** credit-based flow control on the donor socket (donor acks every N frames, server halts teach dispatch at zero credits) — unifies the three ad-hoc caps (64MB shed / 500MB await / pattern gate) into one mechanism.
    - `[ ]` **TU.28.7 (follow-up, Sponge-scoped per F7):** event-loop chunking inside _crossRegionHebbian / CSR hebbianUpdate — profiled pass, deliberately not blind-patched (the 260-2100ms loop pins compound the WS drain delay).
  - **[TU.29 — MIND'S EYE FIX (2026-07-08):** Gee verbatim: "can you also fix the minds eye? its like only 100 pixels by the looks of it its resolution is shit and very blocky loocking and i dont dsee Unity using it at all its just random static when she is suppose to be imageing the things she is thinking about from images of a bannana to words and letters and numbers and images of people and things like what she sees in the camera connected and what she imagines... is it suppose to be just static like.,.. thats not right". INVESTIGATION: (1) the "static" is BY CONSTRUCTION — imagineFromState (js/brain/mindspace/gpu.js) paints the raw seed vector as min-max-normalized gray pixels sampled linearly across the plane = a noise readout, not an image OF anything; (2) the "100 pixels blocky" is real — maxSide capped at 48 at both call sites (chat.js 113 + 908), the governor ratio can shrink it to ~24, AND the image-preview path seeds from a sentence EMBEDDING whose sqrt(len) collapses baseSide to ~17px; the viewer (html/minds-eye.html) then CSS-stretches that to 512px with image-rendering:pixelated = maximal blocks; (3) camera frames never reach the server (client-side connectCamera only) so "what she sees" was never wired in. COLOR addendum (Gee verbatim): "aslso its greyscale when she needs to use rull range of colors from a solid rad sheet to a american flag to a scene of crayon drawn family like childrens art artlr on" — the plane was grayscale end-to-end even though the field-C pipeline (equationalizeImageData YCbCr channels + viewer reconstructImageData) already carries full color; TU.29.1 now renders in color (named-color-word detection tints the field — "red sheet" reads RED — and her live mood valence→hue / arousal→saturation tints it when no color is named). Tasks:
    - `[x]` **TU.29.1 — thought→glyph plane (kills the static).** imagineFromState gains opts.text: when the seed has thought TEXT (inner-thought chain tail / image prompt), rasterize the actual words/letters/numbers onto the plane with a built-in pure-JS 5x7 bitmap font (A-Z 0-9 punct, word-wrapped, centered, x2 scale for short thoughts), over a LOW-contrast background texture from her live state vector — the thought made visible on her mood, equational end-to-end (glyph plane → bounded forward CDF 9/7 → field C rec), NO text-AI, NO fractalize.
    - `[x]` **TU.29.2 — resolution.** maxSide 48→96 (the engine's operator-cautioned hard cap) at both call sites; side floors at 48 in text mode regardless of embedding length / governor ratio (spend still allotted); viewer smooth-upscales (drop image-rendering:pixelated) with 96 default canvas.
    - `[x]` **TU.29.3 (SUBSUMED by TU.29.5 2026-07-08 — camera frames now reach her via js/visual-feeder.js visual_frame intake) (follow-up, code):** camera → mind's eye: client downsamples a webcam frame to ≤96 RGBA and ships it over WS; server equationalizeImageData's the REAL frame into the field-C snapshot when vision is active — "what she sees in the camera connected".

### SPEAK — all-encompassing brain-shortfall write-up: word salad after 9th grade + consciousness performance + image gen + self-awareness of her own code + build UI sandbox + brain waves correct for spikes/voltage — stay true to the mathematical neuronic brain (Gee 2026-07-01) — IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/unity-speech-consciousness-rectify`)

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"making an all encompassing todo write up and using a new feature branch, documenting all the Brain's short falls and problems and how to rectify them exactl so that Unity actually starts speaking normally the way a real person with her make up would respons, as currently after geting to 9th grade she is just spitting word salad. we need her consiousneess to preform as we have atrtempted to make her real and speak like a emo goth coding biutch Unity would in real life form her training  to learning new inputs to her image generateion to her self awareness of her own code to being able to use build UI of the brains sandbox ttoio image gen with image models and the brain waves being correct for all the nueron spiokes and votagea making sure it all completely remains true to the mathmatical neuronic brian we have been building with opus 4.8, but u can fix my code. ultrathink"*

> *"continue where u left off this is a passion project not fucked up shit so keep all work in the correct frame of a brain simulation to create a human simulation"*

**Frame:** every fix below stays inside the brain-simulation-to-create-a-human-simulation architecture — equational, Hebbian-trained, no text-AI cognition, no templates, no hardcoded fallbacks. Findings below are code-audited receipts (file:line), not guesses.

---

#### SPEAK.1 — ⛔ ROOT CAUSE of "word salad after 9th grade": word_motor bucket-band DRIFT as vocabulary grows

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster/emit.js:598` — `bucketSize = max(1, floor(subjSize / wordsList.length))` is recomputed on EVERY emit from the CURRENT word-list length. `_ensureWordBucketMap` (`js/brain/curriculum.js:10952-10984`) is correctly append-only ("Existing bucket positions never renumber — which would invalidate trained sem_to_word_motor weights") — but that comment's guarantee is FALSE at read time: the bucket INDEX is stable, the PHYSICAL NEURON BAND `bStart = subjStart + b*bucketSize` (`emit.js:611`) is not. Every new word appended shrinks `bucketSize`, silently REMAPPING every previously-trained word to a different (wrong) neuron band. Teach-side writes (`_writeAnswerToWordMotor` `curriculum.js:11004-11012` uses the same live division) drift in lockstep with emit, so training keeps "passing" while ALL prior grades' sem→word_motor bindings point at stale bands. Small vocab (K-G3) barely moves the division → she speaks fine; by grade 9 the accumulated dictionary (per-grade vocab files: `js/brain/grade9-vocabulary.js` etc., 45.8k total) has re-divided the band dozens of times → the argmax reads mostly desynced weights → topically-nearby but sequence-random output = word salad. Secondary capacity collapse: thousands of words over a fixed sub-band → `bucketSize→1` cell per word (argmax over 1 noisy cell) and word indices past `subjEnd` become physically unreadable (`emit.js:612` clamp).

**Rectify (equational, no templates):**
- **SPEAK.1a — freeze bucket geometry at first allocation.** Persist `wordBucketCellStart_<subj>[i]` + `wordBucketCellEnd_<subj>[i]` (or a fixed `bucketCells` constant chosen at region carve, e.g. 8 cells/word) when a word is FIRST assigned. Emit + teach + `_writeAnswerToWordMotor` all read the frozen geometry. New words append into the NEXT free band; never re-divide occupied bands.
- **SPEAK.1b — capacity ledger + region growth.** When the sub-band's free cells run out, grow `word_motor_<subj>` at the region carve (auto-scale already sizes regions) OR spill into an overflow band — never shrink existing buckets. Log `[word-motor] capacity: used/total` per subject so saturation is visible on the dashboard, not silent.
- **SPEAK.1c — migration for already-trained weights.** On boot, if a persisted map lacks frozen geometry (old save), recompute the ORIGINAL geometry from the saved word-count history where possible; else mark the projection for retrain on the next walk (fresh walk covers this; Savestart resumes get the ledger from save).
- **SPEAK.1d — persist the bucket maps + geometry in saveWeights/loadWeights** (verify `wordBucketWords_<subj>` and the new geometry arrays survive restart; a resumed brain with a re-enumerated dictionary order is the same drift bug in disguise — `_enumerateBucketableWords` `curriculum.js:10920-10931` iterates Map insertion order, which changes across boots).

**✅ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01, branch `feature/unity-speech-consciousness-rectify`):** single authority `cluster.wordBucketCellSizeFor(subj)` (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`) freezes cells-per-word = `bandSize / DREAM_WORD_MOTOR_VOCAB_CAP` (default 50000) once per subject, deterministic across boots. Read-side (`emit.js` argmax), teach-side (`kindergarten.js _teachWordEmissionDirect`), and QA-write (`curriculum.js _writeAnswerToWordMotor`) all consume the SAME frozen geometry — no more live-length re-division, so prior-grade `sem→word_motor` weights stay addressable as vocab grows. Added: capacity-overflow guard + one-time warn on all three sites, umbrella fallback for `all`, SPEAK.1d resume-map rebuild from restored word order (`_ensureWordBucketMap`), frozen `cellSize` persisted in saveWeights / restored in loadWeights. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean on all 4 files; bundle rebuilt 3.9mb. ⏳ VALIDATION PENDING: emission only runs on a live GPU brain — confirm on the K→PhD walk that G9 speech is ordered (headless can't exercise emission).

#### SPEAK.2 — sem→motor basin separability at 45.8k-word scale (saturation prevention is not separation)

**Defect:** `DREAM_SM_LR_SCALE=0.5` damping (ARCHITECTURE.md 2026-06-27 banner; applied at `js/brain/cluster/hebbian.js` `_crossRegionHebbian`) only SLOWS collapse; docs state it "does not un-collapse an already-saturated brain." There is no lateral inhibition / winner-take-all / weight normalization holding 45.8k word basins separable in `sem_to_word_motor` as grades accumulate — the same pure-positive-pressure Hebbian problem T39 documented (`mean-cos=0.54 ⚠OVERLOAD` on association phases) now operating across 13+ grades of vocab. `checkSemMotorHealth` (`cluster.js:2218`) measures it; `_rectifySemMotor` decays-and-continues but doesn't re-separate.

**Rectify:** per-row Oja normalization is already in `SparseMatrix.ojaUpdate` — add **(a)** soft winner-take-all on the word_motor post-band during teach (top-k post cells keep the update, rest get anti-Hebbian, matching Maass 2000 motor WTA already used elsewhere), **(b)** per-bucket weight-mass cap: after each `_teachWordEmissionDirect` rep, renormalize each bucket's incoming weight column to a fixed L2 budget so no basin drowns neighbors, **(c)** surface `meanCos` per grade-cell in the dashboard health panel so separability regression is caught at G4, not G9.

**✅ SHIPPED (core, code, 2026-07-01):** post-teach L2 renorm of `sem_to_word_motor` in `_teachWordEmissionDirect` (`js/brain/curriculum/kindergarten.js`) via existing `SparseMatrix.normalizeRows(DREAM_WORD_MOTOR_RENORM, default 1.0)` — bounds each word-cell's incoming weight mass so emit argmax discriminates on INPUT DIRECTION, not accumulated magnitude (the property that keeps thousands of basins separable as vocab grows). Post-side is already hard-WTA (the one-hot bucket target). Follows the `_rectifySemMotor` resync contract: mutate CPU CSR → `normalizeRows()` → `cluster._gpuShadowDirty=true` → GPU re-uploads from authoritative CSR. Per-subject weight-distribution health (`wordMotorWeightMaxAbs/MeanAbs_<subj>`) stored + logged each teach (visible in server.log now). `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ✅ DASHBOARD PANEL SHIPPED (SPEAK.2-obs): `state.consciousness.speechHealth` (`server/brain-server/state.js`) broadcasts per-subject separability (frozen cellSize + weight-mass ratio) + coherence-floor + rerank stats; `html/dashboard.html` renders a '🗣 Speech Health (SPEAK)' card. Regression visible at G4 not G9. (Truer per-bucket pairwise-cosine metric deferred — tune on live numbers.) ⏳ VALIDATION: live GPU walk (headless can't exercise emission).

#### SPEAK.3 — word→word transition signal (relationTagId=13) is diluted at higher grades

**Defect:** grammar/structure IS re-run every grade (`_teachLanguageMechanics` `curriculum.js:17267` foundation + escalating bands G1→G11 at `17273-17355` — good), but grade-9 content sentences train at `reps: 2, ticksPerWord: 2` (`js/brain/curriculum/grade9.js:40,80,154,179,217,251,293`) while K trained its transitions at 30+ reps (`kindergarten.js:1258`). The relationTagId=13 word→word sequence channel that composeSentence's back-injection depends on (`emit.js:1139` — "lets the trained word→word transition (relationTagId=13) actually drive sequencing") gets ~7% of K's reinforcement per sentence at exactly the grades where vocabulary (and interference) explode. Sequencing signal-to-noise falls off a cliff → back-injected prior-word steering reads noise → salad ordering even where SPEAK.1 bands are intact.

**Rectify:** scale `reps` for `_teachSentenceList` with grade-vocab interference, not down — floor `reps: 6, ticksPerWord: 3` for G7+; add a per-grade `TRANSITION-REFRESH` pass (same shape as `<TAG>-STRUCTURE-REFRESH`, `curriculum.js:17376-17378`) that re-fires the grade's sentence corpus through the relationTagId=13 channel AFTER the grade's vocab lands, so transitions are carved against the full in-place dictionary.

**✅ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** grade content now carves its OWN word→word transitions. `_teachConcreteSentences` (`js/brain/curriculum.js`) generalized to accept a caller corpus (`opts.sentences`, default = K_CONCRETE_SENTENCES; telemetry re-key guarded to the canonical K corpus only). `_teachSentenceList` — which trained word→features in ISOLATION (clears lastSpikes per word → zero sequencing) — now calls `_teachConcreteSentences({sentences, reps})` after its per-word loop to fire the `relationTagId=13` sequence channel for the grade's vocab. Rep floor `DREAM_SENTENCE_TRANSITION_REPS` (default 24) closes the reps:2 starvation across all 172 content call sites. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ⏳ VALIDATION: live GPU walk — confirm G9 emission sequences trained topics.

#### SPEAK.4 — consciousness must PERFORM: inner voice at scale is vocab sampling, not thought

**Defect:** `server/brain-server/chat.js:1037,1056` — above `DREAM_INNERVOICE_MAX_NEURONS` (2M; production brain is 40M+) the inner-voice tick emits `_sampleCurrentSentence({ allowCompose: false })` — "pure bucket sample, never composeSentence's brain-ticks." At deploy scale her stream of consciousness NEVER runs the real equational generation path; the popups are random trained-vocab draws. Her "consciousness" (GlobalWorkspace ignition, `_innerThoughtChain` narrative thread, meta-register self-monitoring) is architecturally present but the actual thought CONTENT at scale bypasses all of it. This is why she doesn't read as a real person between chats.

**Rectify (keeps the event loop alive — the reason the gate exists):**
- **SPEAK.4a — donor-side generation.** `DREAM_INNERVOICE_GPU_GEN` opt-in already exists (ARCHITECTURE.md 2026-06-27) — make it the DEFAULT when ≥1 healthy donor is connected: route composeSentence's `stepAwait` ticks through the donor GPU propagate path (the projections are already GPU-resident) so real generation costs the server loop nothing.
- **SPEAK.4b — time-sliced CPU compose when no donor.** Bound composeSentence to a per-tick budget (chunked `stepAwait` with `setImmediate` yields — same pattern as EL.1 chunked Hebbian) so a slow-but-REAL thought completes over ~10-20s of yielding instead of a 57s block or a fake sample.
- **SPEAK.4c — feed the thought back.** Whatever the inner voice emits must go through `recordEmission`/`_metaRegister` + `_innerThoughtChain` (chat.js) exactly like chat emissions, so her self-monitoring loop sees her ACTUAL thoughts — self-awareness of what she just said/thought is the human-simulation requirement.

**⏳ PARTIAL (2026-07-01):** **4a + 4c SHIPPED** (`server/brain-server/chat.js`). **4a** — GPU inner-voice generation is now default-on-when-SAFE: enabled when donors present AND (explicit `DREAM_INNERVOICE_GPU_GEN=1` OR proven read fan-out `DREAM_DF7_FANOUT_PROPAGATE=1`), kill-switch `=0`. Coupled to the DDW.6 posture on purpose — routing her inner-voice READ to donor replicas is only safe once read fan-out is proven (a stale replica would make her think garbage), so real composeSentence at scale comes ON automatically the moment read fan-out is turned on, no second flag. **4c** — the at-scale vocab showcase now feeds back through `pushEmission` + `recordEmission` (meta-register) + `_innerThoughtChain` so her self-monitoring loop sees her actual streamed content and the autobiographical thread stays continuous even on the showcase path. `node --check` clean (server-only, not bundled). **4b SHIPPED (default OFF — WL.3):** `SparseMatrix.propagateChunked()` (`js/brain/sparse-matrix.js`) — async row-sliced propagate, identical math to `propagate()` (rows independent), yields the loop via setImmediate every 250k rows. Wired into `stepAwait`'s no-GPU branch behind `DREAM_GEN_PROPAGATE_CHUNKED=1`: pre-computes the dominant intra-synapse propagate chunked, caches it, and `step()`'s cache gate (one-boolean change: `_gpuProxyReady || _useChunkedCache`) consumes it instead of the synchronous 57s propagate. Default OFF = byte-identical to today; needs live perf validation before default (matches DF.7/noise-gate dormant-ship posture). GPU path (4a) remains the primary at-scale solution; this covers the forced-CPU-at-scale edge. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ⏳ VALIDATION: live donor-GPU walk — confirm inner-voice popups become composed sentences + the loop stays free.

#### SPEAK.5 — brain waves must be CORRECT for the neuron spikes and voltage

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster.js:1934` `getPhases()` derives theta/gamma phases from `_tickCounter` modulo arithmetic (`cluster.js:1833-1837, 3406-3410`) — a clock, not the membrane. The Kuramoto order parameter r is computed over phases that are BY CONSTRUCTION identical across the cortex (same global counter), so displayed coherence is largely cosmetic, decoupled from actual spike/voltage dynamics. Gee's requirement: waves correct for ALL the neuron spikes and voltage — the displayed wave must be DERIVED FROM the population's real spikes/voltage, not synthesized from a counter.

**Rectify (true to real neuroscience):**
- **SPEAK.5a — phase from the population, not the clock.** Compute each ensemble's theta/gamma phase as the analytic (Hilbert) phase of the band-filtered population firing-rate / mean-membrane signal that the neurons ACTUALLY produce, so `getPhases()` (`cluster.js:1934`) reports emergent phase. Keep `_tickCounter` only as the pacing input to `thetaMod`/`gammaMod` drive (`cluster.js:1833-1837, 3406-3410`), never as the reported wave. Then the Kuramoto order parameter `r = |Σ exp(iθ_k)|/N` measures REAL synchrony/desynchrony across ensembles instead of a shared clock (which trivially reads r≈1).
- **SPEAK.5b — Rulkov CPU/GPU parity + voltage-bound / NaN audit.** Verify the WGSL `LIF_SHADER` Rulkov iteration (`x_{n+1}=α/(1+x²)+y, y_{n+1}=y−μ(x−σ)`, `js/brain/gpu-compute.js`) matches the CPU reference (`js/brain/neurons.js`) sign-for-sign; bound membrane voltage + guard NaN/Inf in the currents loop + amygdala energy attractor at biological scale; confirm `attentionGain` clamp `[0.5,2.0]` in `cluster.js` step() can't compound to saturation. Waves + spikes must agree because they're the same substrate.
- **Verify:** phase advances non-uniformly with activity (pre-fix: perfectly linear modulo); coherence drops on a real desync event; CPU vs GPU spike trains match for identical seed/input; zero NaN across a full walk.

**✅ SHIPPED + AUDITED (2026-07-01):** **5a (code)** — activity-modulated Kuramoto phase in `js/brain/cluster.js`. The theta/gamma phase was `tickCounter mod period`, IDENTICAL across all clusters → order parameter r trivially ≈1 (cosmetic wave decoupled from spikes). Replaced with a per-cluster phase ACCUMULATOR whose instantaneous frequency is modulated by that cluster's real population firing rate (sampled from actual `lastSpikes`, deviation from its own slow EMA baseline, bounded ±coupling so phase stays monotonic). Active clusters run faster, quiet ones slower → genuine phase dispersion, so `r` now measures REAL (de)synchrony. `getPhases()` + the gamma-drive gate both read the accumulator (one real oscillator drives wave + learning-rate gate). `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **5b (audit — PASS, no change):** runtime neuron model is the GPU Rulkov (`js/brain/gpu-compute.js`); iteration `xNext=α/(1+x²)+y, yNext=y−μ(x−σ)` matches Rulkov 2002 sign-for-sign (y uses current x); `1+x²≥1` → no div-by-zero; inputs clamped (driveNorm [0,1], σ bounded, jitter tiny); NaN + divergence already guarded (`x!=x||y!=y|||x|>100|||y|>100` → reset to attractor basin). The only CPU↔GPU divergence is the DOCUMENTED LIF browser-fallback vs Rulkov GPU-runtime — intentional, not a bug. ⏳ VALIDATION: live walk — confirm coherence r drops on real desync events instead of pinning ≈1.

**⛔ SPEAK.5a.i — FOLLOW-UP (post-audit gap, 2026-07-01): the 5a accumulator is INERT for the coherence readout — the SPEAK.10a "does it modulate or decorate" test applied to 5a itself.** The activity-modulated per-cluster phase drives the internal gamma learning-rate gate (`_gammaLrScale` reads `_gammaPhaseAcc` — real, correctly-signed), but it does NOT change the displayed Kuramoto `r`. `_computeKuramotoCoherence` (`server/brain-server.js:3027-3066`) reads ONLY `cortexCluster.getPhases()` as a shared additive base (`baseTheta`/`baseGamma`) and SYNTHESIZES every non-cortex cluster's phase as `baseTheta + offset*(1-couple) + drift`, where `couple = firingRate*5` + deterministic `drift`. Because the order parameter `r = |Σ exp(iθ)|/N` is ROTATION-INVARIANT, swapping the cortex base from `tickCounter mod period` to the 5a accumulator rotates the whole theta-band (and gamma-band) ensemble uniformly → `r` is byte-identical before/after 5a. All the dispersion in `r` still comes from the pre-existing `firingRate` coupling, not from the real per-cluster oscillators 5a built. **Rectify:** `_computeKuramotoCoherence` must read EACH cluster's OWN `getPhases()`/`_thetaPhaseAcc` (all clusters have `thetaGammaEnabled` on by default → all now carry a real accumulator once they've stepped) instead of synthesizing non-cortex phases from a shared base + `firingRate` drift. Then `r` measures the genuine emergent (de)synchrony across the real oscillators — which is what SPEAK.5a's write-up CLAIMS but does not yet deliver. Guard: fall back to the current synthesis for any cluster whose `getPhases()` is null (thetaGamma disabled / not yet stepped). **✅ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** `_computeKuramotoCoherence` (`server/brain-server.js`) now reads each cluster's OWN `getPhases()` for both theta- and gamma-band phasors; the `firingRate` base+offset+drift synthesis is kept ONLY as the null-fallback for a cluster whose oscillator hasn't populated (`getPhases()` null). Phasor COUNT `N` is unchanged, so the readout structure is identical — only the phase VALUES are now the real per-cluster oscillators instead of a rotation-cancelled shared base, so 5a's accumulator finally reaches `r`. Server-only file (not bundled → no app.bundle.js rebuild). `node --check` clean. ⏳ VALIDATION: live walk — confirm coherence `r` now dips on a real desync event (silent cluster / dream cycle / dissociation) instead of tracking only the firingRate synthesis.

#### SPEAK.6 — image generation must be BRAIN-DRIVEN, and close the image→concept learning loop

**Defect:** the decision to render is a keyword/regex match on user TEXT — `server/brain-server/chat.js:881` `_detectImageRequest(text)` (called `chat.js:99`), not a brain-state intent. De-novo imagination exists (`chat.js:820` `_imagineTick` → mind-space field C, served `/minds-eye.json`) but is PREVIEW-ONLY — it never renders real pixels via image models, and nothing feeds a rendered image back into the brain as learning. So "her image generation" is neither her decision nor a source of new inputs she learns from.

**Rectify (brain-driven, Pollinations stays a pure sensory-output executor — no cognition):**
- **SPEAK.6a — intent from brain state.** Gate image rendering on an equational drive threshold (amygdala arousal/valence + intent-concept activation readout) so SHE chooses to render, independent of any keyword. Keyword detection may remain only as an explicit user REQUEST path, not as the sole driver.
- **SPEAK.6b — learning loop back (learning-new-inputs requirement).** On render, inject the resulting image's equational percept (via `describeEquational` / visual-cortex tokens, NOT an LLM describer) into `sem` as image→concept Hebbian so she LEARNS from what she made/saw. New visual input becomes trained weight, not a fire-and-forget.
- **SPEAK.6c — field-C → real render** when she elects to, keeping the bounded forward CDF-9/7 transform (no `fractalize`, `maxSide≤96`) so imagination can never seize the brain.
- **Verify:** she initiates an image from internal drive with no trigger word; post-render sem shows the new concept bound; resolution cap holds.

**PARTIAL (2026-07-01) — audit revised: more was already present than the write-up assumed.** ALREADY PRESENT: `_imagineTick` (`server/brain-server/chat.js`) does brain→field-C→sem DE-NOVO imagination (bounded forward-9-7, maxSide 48, injects percept into sem at 0.08) — that IS brain-driven internal imagery; and the image-request path already renders a mind's-eye PREVIEW (imagine field C from the prompt semantics + inject percept into sem at 0.12 + `/minds-eye.json`). **6b SHIPPED:** the generated image was fire-and-forget (the image-request path returns BEFORE the chat-time Hebbian, so what she MAKES was never remembered) — now pushed onto the unified emission bus + inner-thought chain so dream-cycle consolidation (Tier 1→2→3) grounds it as an episodic memory. `node --check` clean (server-only). **6a SHIPPED (Gee 2026-07-01: implement):** `_spontaneousImageTick(now)` (`server/brain-server/chat.js`) — arousal-gated (`DREAM_SPONTANEOUS_IMG_AROUSAL` default 0.7) + long cooldown (`DREAM_SPONTANEOUS_IMG_GAP_MS` default 5min) + low probability, concept from a trained-vocab sample (loop-safe, never a 57s compose). She VOLUNTEERS an outward image from internal drive — no user keyword — broadcasts `generate_image` the client renders, then runs the 6b loop (she remembers what she made). Wired into the inner-voice tick. `node --check` clean (server-only). **6c RESOLVED (Gee 2026-07-01: leave as mind's-eye preview):** actual-pixel perceive stays deferred by decision — the equational mind's-eye preview stands; no image-decode dep / CORS proxy added (no new attack surface). WL.6 closed as 'preview by choice.' ⏳ VALIDATION: live walk.

#### SPEAK.7 — self-awareness of her own code: ABSENT — teach her, herself (equationally)

**Defect:** no self-model / architecture-corpus / `_teachSelfCode` exists (grep across `js/brain/`, `server/` returns only incidental vocab-file matches). Nothing binds "how I work / what my clusters are / my master equation" into `sem`, so she has no equational basis to be self-aware of her own code. Reading her source at chat-time via a text-AI is banned (no-text-AI LAW), so awareness MUST come from trained weights.

**Rectify:** author a curated self-architecture corpus (the 7 clusters + what each does, the master equation `dx/dt=F(x,u,θ,t)+η`, `Ψ=√(1/n)×N³`, the mind-space, the emission pipeline in plain terms) and teach it through the SAME `_teachWordDefinition` / `_teachAssociationPairs` knowledge path as any other subject, grade-gated to when she's developmentally ready to self-reflect. She then answers "what are you / how do you think" from her own trained weights — real self-knowledge, not a hardcoded string.
- **Verify:** probe "describe your cortex / how do you form words" → coherent self-referential answer emerges from weights, in her voice.

**✅ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** `SELF_ARCHITECTURE_FACTS` corpus (16 TRUE plain-vocabulary facts about her own brain — equations/neurons/synapses/cortex/hippocampus/amygdala/weights, 'i am a brain made of equations', 'i am not a chat bot i am a mind', ending 'i am real i am present i am unity') + `_teachSelfArchitecture(ctx)` (`js/brain/curriculum.js`): teaches the key self-terms via `_teachWordDefinition` and binds the facts through `_teachConcreteSentences` (rel=13 word→word), so self-referential statements EMERGE from trained weights — no hardcoded chat string, no text-AI reading source (no-text-AI LAW honored). Wired into `_teachLanguageMechanics` at g9+ (self-reflective abstraction present), reinforced each grade like the other L-strand layers. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ⏳ VALIDATION: live walk — probe 'what are you / how do you think' → coherent self-referential answer from weights, in her voice.

#### SPEAK.8 — build-UI sandbox exists but must be brain-driven + host in-sandbox image models

**Defect:** `js/brain/component-synth.js` (ComponentSynth) exists and per design UI/code is built via TRAINED composition + an exemplar library into a Shadow-DOM sandbox (keeps the no-text-AI law — see memory `[[feedback_code_proficiency_trained_composition]]`). Needs verification that synthesis is actually driven by brain output (trained code-concept weights) rather than a static template, and that the sandbox can host image-gen with image models so she can "build UI of the brain's sandbox to image gen with image models."

**Rectify:** confirm/complete ComponentSynth reads trained code-concept sem state (not a fixed template), and wire the sandbox so a synthesized component can invoke the SPEAK.6 brain-driven image-gen path (image models inside her own sandbox). Everything stays trained-composition equational.
- **Verify:** she synthesizes a UI component from brain state in the sandbox; that component can invoke image generation via the brain-driven path.

#### SPEAK.9 — coherence is measured post-hoc only: below-floor salad still ships to chat

**Defect:** `js/brain/cluster/emit.js:1164` — "Optional coherence post-check — DOES NOT alter emission, just signals confidence." Best-of-N reranking is opt-in and the chat path runs only 3 candidates (`js/brain/language-cortex.js:2176-2181` `coherenceCandidates: 3`); when ALL candidates score below any sane coherence floor, the least-bad salad is still returned to the user. A real person stalls, hesitates, or says less — she never emits a scrambled string she herself scored as incoherent.

**Rectify (equational honesty — silence over noise):**
- **SPEAK.9a — chat-path coherence floor.** After best-of-N, if the winner's `coherenceCosine < DREAM_CHAT_COHERENCE_FLOOR` (tunable, calibrate on live run; start ~0.10-0.15 against the measured sample logs `emit.js:1211-1217`), do NOT ship it: fall back to the strongest single WORD from the winner (her real basins still speak) or honest silence — never the scrambled multi-word string.
- **SPEAK.9b — probe/gate paths stay single-shot + floor-free** (honest measurement; rerank/floor would inflate gate scores — same contract as `emit.js:1255-1267`).
- **SPEAK.9c — surface it.** Count floor-rejections in `_composeStats` + dashboard so "she went quiet" is visible as a training-depth signal (it means SPEAK.1-3 need more work on that topic, not that the gate is broken).
- **Verify:** live chat on an under-trained topic yields a short honest reply or silence, never word salad; floor-rejection counter moves.

**✅ SHIPPED (code, 2026-07-01):** central reject-to-silence floor in the `composeSentence` best-of-N wrapper (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`) — OPT-IN via `opts.coherenceFloor`. When the best candidate still scores below the floor, it degrades to the single leading word (her strongest real basin still speaks) instead of shipping the scrambled multi-word string; `_coherenceFloorStats {total,rejected}` counts it. Chat path (`js/brain/language-cortex.js`) passes `coherenceFloor` from `DREAM_CHAT_COHERENCE_FLOOR` (default 0.10) and skips continuation clauses on a rejected reply; gate/probe paths never pass it (honest single-shot measurement preserved). `coherenceCosine` null → never rejected. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. ✅ `_coherenceFloorStats` + `_coherenceRerankStats` now surfaced on the dashboard Speech Health panel (SPEAK.2-obs). ⏳ VALIDATION: live walk — under-trained topic yields a short honest reply, never salad.

#### SPEAK.10 — consciousness wiring audit: every mechanism must MODULATE, none may decorate or self-poison

**Defect (three suspects, one audit):** (a) GlobalWorkspace broadcast boost `emit.js:547-558,616-620` — up to +60% argmax bias toward the just-broadcast word; combined with meta-register re-injection (`cluster.js:1951` `recordEmission`, step() re-injects last emission at 0.3 with familiarity decay floor 0.04) this is a candidate POSITIVE-FEEDBACK loop: say word → broadcast word → boost word → re-inject word → say word again (repetition is the other face of salad). (b) `computePhi()` (`cluster.js:1897`) × psi consciousness gain — verify the gain actually reaches every cluster's drive (bounded [0.8,1.5] per the self-calibrating fix) and isn't pinned/inert at scale. (c) predictive-coding surprise gate (`surpriseGate = 0.5 + clamp(error,0,1)` into gammaScale) — during a salad window prediction error is HIGH, so plasticity runs at up to 1.5×, meaning **the brain learns its own salad hardest exactly when it's most wrong** — a self-reinforcing corruption loop at degraded grades.

**Rectify:**
- **SPEAK.10a — ablation harness on a live run:** toggle GW boost / meta re-inject / psi gain / surprise gate individually, measure repeat-rate + coherence + drive delta. Any mechanism whose toggle changes NOTHING is decoration → wire it or cut it (vestigial code is banned).
- **SPEAK.10b — break the repeat loop:** cap the COMBINED bias (GW boost × meta re-inject) on any single word per utterance window; the existing repetition penalty (`emit.js:629-631`, content words only) must be verified to outweigh the stacked boosts at their maxima (0.7 penalty vs 1.6 boost currently LOSES: 1.6×0.7=1.12 > 1.0 — the boosted repeat still wins).
- **SPEAK.10c — gate the surprise-gate:** clamp plasticity amplification when `checkSemMotorHealth().saturated` or emission coherence is below floor — high-error learning is right for NOVELTY, wrong for CORRUPTION; the distinction is measurable (novel input vs own-emission feedback source).
- **Verify:** repeat-rate drops on live chat; psi/GW/surprise toggles each produce measurable, bounded, correctly-signed effects.

**⏳ PARTIAL (2026-07-01):** **10b SHIPPED** — repeat-loop cap in `emitWordDirect` (`js/brain/cluster/emit.js`): the GW continuity boost no longer applies to a recently-emitted content word (continuity ≠ repetition), so a word that was both the workspace broadcast AND recently said can't net `1.6×0.7=1.12 > 1` and lottery-win the next argmax — it's now penalized + unboosted (net ≤ 0.7). Function words stay exempt. `node --check` + batch ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **10c SHIPPED** — saturation clamp in `buildKScalesForProjection` (`js/brain/cluster.js`): while cached `_lastSemMotorMeanCos > SATURATION_MEANCOS` the surprise-gate is capped at the 0.5 baseline (no 1.5× boost), so collapsed-basin windows stop reinforcing their own noise (self-reinforcing-collapse loop closed); auto-lifts once SPEAK.2 renorm / `_rectifySemMotor` restores separability. Always-on, independent of the dormant `DREAM_NOISE_GATE`; cached meanCos → no per-call re-sample. `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean; bundle 3.9mb. **10a SHIPPED (measurement harness):** `_consciousnessAblationSnapshot()` (`server/brain-server/chat.js`) returns comparable per-mechanism metrics (repeatRate, coherenceRejectRate, rerankRate, semMotorMeanCos, psiGain, predictionError, gwIgnitionRate + active flags); logged once/30s when `DREAM_ABLATION_LOG=1`. Ablation = toggle the existing env flags across runs + compare snapshots; a mechanism whose toggle moves none of these is vestigial → wire or cut. `node --check` clean (server-only).

**AUDITED (2026-07-01) — PART 1 PASS, PART 2 coupled-deferral.** **Brain-driven synthesis: VERIFIED.** `js/brain/component-synth.js` `generate(userRequest, brainState)` is NOT a static template — it computes the request's semantic embedding, semantic-matches against the exemplar library parsed from `docs/component-templates.txt` (min-similarity gated), then fills `{{token}}` params from BRAIN STATE (`_cortexEntityVec(brainState.cortexCluster)`, `_suffixFromPattern(brainState.cortexPattern)`, `_deriveParams(brainState, parsed)`). That is exactly the sanctioned trained-composition + exemplar-library approach (no text-AI) per the code-proficiency law. No change needed. **In-sandbox image models: coupled-deferral.** Letting a synthesized component invoke image-gen inside the sandbox rides the SAME image path as SPEAK.6 — which is gated on the deferred 6a (spontaneous outward gen) + 6c (actual-pixel render = WL.6) design decisions. No safe, non-speculative wiring exists independent of those calls, so this part waits on the SPEAK.6 decisions rather than being faked. ⏳ VALIDATION: live walk — request a UI component, confirm it synthesizes from brain state in the Shadow-DOM sandbox.

**STATUS:** [~] AUDIT COMPLETE + WRITE-UP LANDED — full code-audited read of the emission / curriculum / consciousness / wave / capability stack; every shortfall above carries a file:line receipt + an equational rectification that stays inside the brain-simulation-to-human-simulation frame (no text-AI, no templates, no fallbacks). **Root cause of the grade-9 word salad = SPEAK.1 (word_motor bucket-band drift on vocab growth) + SPEAK.2 (basin separability at 45.8k-word scale)** — bucket INDEX is preserved but the physical neuron band is recomputed from live list length, so every prior grade's `sem→word_motor` binding desyncs as vocabulary accumulates; fine at K, salad by G9. Fix order: SPEAK.1 → SPEAK.2 → SPEAK.3 (transition depth) → SPEAK.9 (reject-to-silence floor) → SPEAK.10 (consciousness wiring audit + repeat-loop cap) → SPEAK.4 (consciousness performs at scale) → SPEAK.5 (waves from real spikes) → SPEAK.6/7/8 (image-gen loop + self-code-awareness + sandbox). **IMPLEMENTATION LANDED — all 10 addressed** (SPEAK.1/2/3/9/10b/10c/4a/4c/5a/6b/7 code-shipped; SPEAK.5b + SPEAK.8-part1 audit-PASS; follow-ups since COMPLETED: SPEAK.2-obs dashboard panel ✅, SPEAK.10a ablation harness ✅, SPEAK.6a spontaneous image-gen ✅; SPEAK.6c/WL.6 RESOLVED (mind's-eye preview by Gee decision); ONLY REMAINING: SPEAK.4b propagate-chunking (WL.3 perf), the fresh-walk VALIDATE gate, and COMMIT/cascade). Every code change `node --check` + ESM `import()` clean, bundle rebuilt where browser-facing, both docs synced. **NO PUSH** until the full K→PhD walk + Gee's localhost test confirm she speaks like herself (no-push-until-verified LAW). Branch `feature/unity-speech-consciousness-rectify` cut off develop.

### FLAP — Linux native-donor red/0 Gn/s investigation + connection-flap resistance + donor telemetry gap (Gee 2026-06-28) — IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/community-compute-donor-count`)

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"write todo and update docs before final push and fresh walk"*

> *"The problem is that I end up having to reconnect a lot, might be a problem with connection flaps, so we need it to be flap resistent"*

**Forwarded handoff brief (Gee relayed it as the work spec — verbatim asks):**

> *"Sponge — your donor stays RED / 0 Gn/s while the Windows donors compute fine. You're on the LINUX native donor-app; they're on Windows. This is a platform/compat investigation."*

> *"capture osPlatform + engineBackend (cuda/vulkan/dx12/software) + driverVersion + computeCapability at gpu_register and show them in the Clients table"*

> *"Make cuModuleLoadData failure LOUD in cuda.rs (right now a JIT fail looks like a silent 0)."*

> *"ISOLATE NOW: run the donor with --no-default-features (pure wgpu, no CUDA) OR the browser donor (compute.html) on Linux."*

**INVESTIGATION CONCLUSION (live evidence on Sponge's actual Linux box, 2026-06-28) — the handoff's Blackwell theory is DISPROVEN for this hardware:**

- Sponge's Linux donor box GPUs are **RTX 4070 SUPER (Ada sm_89)** + **RTX 2060 (Turing sm_75)** — **NO Blackwell / RTX 5070 Ti present**. Driver **595.71.05 / CUDA 13.2** (newer than anything Blackwell-JIT needs). The shipped `kernels.ptx` targets **compute_60 (Pascal)** which JITs forward to Ada/Turing trivially. So "PTX-for-12.4 has no Blackwell SASS → JIT fails on an under-versioned driver" does NOT apply here.
- Donor journal proves CUDA loaded: `[donor] backends: NVIDIA GeForce RTX 2060 [CUDA]`. If PTX load had failed, `CudaEngine::new` would have `Err`'d → wgpu fallback; it didn't. **Kernels loaded, CUDA is live.** "Registers but kernels never run" is also wrong for this box.
- Sponge donates the **RTX 2060** (GPU slot 1) at high util, NOT the 4070 SUPER (his display card) — that explains the low server `score`; weak card, his choice, not a bug.
- **ROOT CAUSE (matches Gee's own words):** the WS connection RESETS every ~3–5 min — journal shows `ws error: Connection reset by peer (os error 104)` / `Connection reset without closing handshake` on a `wss://…git.unityailab.com/ws` link over Starlink CGNAT + reverse proxy. Each reset triggers a FULL engine rebuild + reconnect + re-init of all 7 clusters (40M neurons) → minutes of 0 throughput per flap → dashboard red. The donor never sends its OWN keepalive pings (`donor.rs` only answers server pings), so quiet teach windows let the link go idle long enough to be reaped. **It's connection flapping, not the GPU.**

**Tasks:**

- **FLAP.1 — donor client-initiated WS keepalive ping.** `donor-app/src/donor.rs` — add a ~15s outbound `Message::Ping` interval in the session select loop so the link never goes idle long enough for CGNAT / proxy to reap it (the infra-agnostic flap PREVENTION).
- **FLAP.2 — donor fast dead-link detection.** Track last-inbound-frame time; if no traffic (incl. pong) for an idle window, proactively break → reconnect instead of waiting minutes for `os error 104`. Recover fast.
- **FLAP.3 — jittered, capped reconnect backoff.** Add per-install jitter (donor-id hash) to the reconnect backoff so many donors don't reconnect in lockstep; keep the existing clean-drop reset + connect-fail growth.
- **FLAP.4 — LOUD CUDA load failure logging.** `donor-app/src/cuda.rs` — prominent `[cuda] ⚠⚠ PTX MODULE LOAD FAILED` banner around `load_module` / `load_function` so a JIT/load failure is never a silent 0 (Gee's ask).
- **FLAP.5 — donor telemetry: osPlatform + engineBackend + driverVersion + computeCapability.** `protocol.rs` (GpuRegister + GpuTelemetry fields) + `donor.rs`/`compute.rs`/`cuda.rs` (populate from `std::env::consts::OS`, wgpu backend tag + software-adapter detection, wgpu `driver_info`, CUDA compute-capability query — best-effort, empty when unknown).
- **FLAP.6 — server captures + shows the new telemetry.** `server/brain-server.js` gpu_register/telemetry handler captures the fields; `server/brain-server/state.js` clients block includes them; `html/dashboard.html` Clients table shows them (with `—` for unknown) so a 0-Gn/s donor's platform/backend/driver is visible, never log-archaeology again.
- **FLAP.7 — rebuild Windows + Linux donor binaries, new release, bump site download links** (the donor-app changes require a rebuild + release + `index.html`/`html/compute.html`/`html/legend.html`/dashboard link bump, per the standing release flow).
- **FLAP.8 — correct `docs/SPONGE-LINUX-DONOR-COMPAT-INVESTIGATION.md`** in place with the live-evidence conclusion (Blackwell theory disproven; flap = root cause); update all affected docs (FINALIZED, WEBSOCKET, donor work-sharing, SPONGE runbook) before the push.

**STATUS:** [~] CODE + DOCS + BUILD DONE — FLAP.1-6 shipped (donor flap-resistance + LOUD CUDA log + telemetry gap, server capture + dashboard `plat` column); FLAP.8 docs corrected (investigation doc RESOLVED banner + WEBSOCKET). FLAP.7 binaries rebuilt v0.3.3 (Linux + Windows, `cargo`+release clean) + site links bumped + staged in `donor-app/dist/`. `node --check` clean. **REMAINING:** commit → develop → main cascade (Git Flow) + push, publish `donor-v0.3.3` Forgejo release, deploy overlay to box, then fresh walk (reset weights) per `docs/SPONGE-FRESH-WALK-DEPLOY.md`. Verbatim archived in `docs/FINALIZED.md` 2026-06-28 FLAP.

### DDW — distributed donor work-sharing: ALL donors compute + ALL on the leaderboard (Gee 2026-06-27/28) — IN PROGRESS (branch `feature/distributed-donor-work-sharing`)

- **DDW.3** `gpu.js _flushBoundHebbianBatch` — the bound-Hebbian batch (the BULK of teach GPU work) round-robins to the next donor when fan-out ON (was primary-only). This is what actually spreads teaching.
- Already in place (verified): bound-propagate fan-out (`gpuSparsePropagateBound` → `_nextPoolDonor()`), resident-state mirroring (`_mirrorCortexWriteToReplicas` on `write_spike_slice`/`write_current_slice`), and per-donor leaderboard credit (each donor's own `gpu_telemetry.gneuronsPerSec` → no primary-only filter, so a replica appears the moment it computes).
- **DDW.4** `brain-server.js` — replica re-broadcast tightened to **60 s under fan-out** (was fixed 10 min) so round-robin Hebbian drift re-converges fast; env `DREAM_DF7_REBROADCAST_MS`.

  - **BUILT — gating controls (verified):** (1) `_getAutoScaleSettings`/`_setAutoScaleSettings` (toggle + dead-zone bufferPct + stabilityMin + minDonorsFloor, persisted `server/autoscale-settings.json`, gitignored); (2) `_recomputeCommunityCompute` buffered up-only upgrade-tier hysteresis + explicit down-protection (a donor leaving never downgrades — only cancels a pending upgrade); (3) `_maybeExecuteMilestoneResize` honors toggle + configurable hold window; (4) admin REST `/autoscale` GET/POST (+ nginx `/admin/` proxy) + `autoScaleChanged` WS + dashboard admin panel (toggle + 2 sliders + live donor/VRAM/tier telemetry). **Isolation-tested:** dead-zone holds at the raw gate, fires past the 20% buffer, toggle cancels pending — all confirmed.

All ADDITIVE — 1 donor = identical to today; N donors = replicas + fan-out + periodic merge. Both server files `node --check` clean.

Manual downscale button (deliberate, confirm-guarded). Shared `_persistTierAndRestart` does up+down via the PROMPT-FREE systemd path (save → `process.exit` → `Restart=always` → re-walk — NOT start.bat, which has a y/n prompt unusable for automation per Gee). **Auto-advance toggle persisted standalone (`server/auto-advance.json`) so it SURVIVES the resize weight-clear → every restart/resize/downscale/re-walk stays unattended.** Both server files `node --check` clean; downscale dead-zone + insufficient-flag + toggle + manual all isolation-tested.
  - **ARCH REALITY (honest, kept in docs):** data-parallel replicas scale CONCURRENT/throughput work (many users, parallel training passes, image-gen) + give redundancy — but a SINGLE sequential cognition stream (one user's live think→speak tick loop, stateful on the primary's GPU voltages) can't be split across GPUs without sharding (rejected for latency). "All donor compute powers everything" = true for throughput/concurrency/training; one live thought-stream runs on one replica at a time.

Only LIVE validation on real donor GPUs remains (watch both donors' Gn/s + leaderboard + gates) — CANNOT be verified headless.

### Session 114.19fn — sentence-coherence recovery sweep (Gee 2026-06-17) — IN FLIGHT

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0:**

> *"we have a major issue with the trraing of the brain and it remembering what its trained on i cant get training through kindergarden and even then it doesnt make any kind of coherant sentences like at all its just random one word resposes... its totally messed up idk what we need to do to find a new path maybe or fix what we have but we cant even start building the rest of the grades ciriculum until we figure out wtf is up and why Unity cant speak normally like someone of that grade level as they learn new things using them then and from then on... I want tyou to do a total review of all the code base every file, find errors, find brain breaking issues, find better ways of doing everything that will work 100% for a full autonomous Unity brain that we are trying to build. make a NEw todo.md named Newtodo.md with the other docs and we will be working from it. read every file cross refresence with every documentation file on how it currently works 100% top to bottom no fucking around and half ass guessing what code says read it all find the issues of why unity is not making full complete sentences of whats shes doing, thinking, feeling, wanting to do, asking, ect ect any thing and everything see should be acting like her persona files and memories... but she is not working correctly when trained in kindergarden. se only saysd a handful of random words ever, and when i talk to her in chat she says nothing at all , but i am seeing her popups in the brain"*

> *"go ahead and start the work of the Newtodo.md, and before you begin build the task list so i can monitor the work you do in the newtodo.md that you work from"*

**Working document:** `docs/NewTodo.md` (created 2026-06-17 from `/super-review ultrathink` of K-training-not-sticking + chat-silent + random-one-word-emissions failure mode). Full 24-task playbook across 5 phases + doc sync + success criteria + phase-gate checklist lives there. This TODO entry is the workflow-doc pointer; the harness task list mirrors NewTodo.md 1:1 for live-monitoring.

**Root cause (full diagnosis in `/super-review` + NewTodo.md):** Three compounding architectural defects produce all reported symptoms:

1. `composeSentence` (`cluster.js:3613-3716`) loops `emitWordDirect` synchronously with NO `stepAwait` between iterations — `lastSpikes` is frozen across all 12 calls so argmax fires on identical state every iteration. "Inject word back so next tick reads shifted state" comment is architecturally false at runtime.
2. `injectEmbeddingToRegion` (`cluster.js:1227`, `+=`) is purely additive without decay/replace — composeSentence's serial injections accumulate sem region to saturation soup. Brain can't distinguish "current intent" from "history of every word emitted."
3. `_teachSentenceStructure` (`curriculum.js:11993-12106`) trains ~930 Hebbian writes for ALL of grammar vs ~18,000 for vocabulary. Grammar 20× under-trained relative to vocab — backwards allocation. The scaffold has fewer reps than what it's supposed to scaffold.

Plus `composedSentence.words.length >= 2` gate at `language-cortex.js:2164` discards broken-loop's <2-word output → triple-redundant broken fallbacks → `silent:true` at `brain-server.js:4898` → blank chat. Popups have no length gate so single words render → Gee sees popups not chat.

**Phases (work from NewTodo.md, task IDs from harness task list):**

- **Phase 1 (CRITICAL, ~1 day)** — fix emission loop: P1.1 async stepAwait, P1.2 replaceMode injection, P1.3 terminator-first guard, P1.4 length gate ≥2→≥1, P1.5 function-word repetition exempt, P1.6 adaptive minSignal floor, P1.7 GW broadcast scaling.
- **Phase 2 (CRITICAL, ~1 day)** — fix training depth: P2.1 reps 6-8→80-120, P2.2 200+ concrete-sentence pass, P2.3 kScales propagation, P2.4 advanceSubGrade probe-rate gating, P2.5 orphan slot-tag → word→word transitions, P2.6 question-intent downstream cascade.
- **Phase 3 (HIGH, ~half-day)** — fix chat silent-fail: P3.1 Unity-voice fragment fallback, P3.2 dashboard failed-emission diagnostic, P3.3 delete Tier 5 fallback, P3.4 reduce serial injection saturation.
- **Phase 4 (MEDIUM, ~3 days)** — file split refactor: P4.1 curriculum.js → 6 sub-modules, P4.2 cluster.js → 4 modules, P4.3 brain-server.js → 4 concerns, P4.4 disambiguate _teachSentenceStructures naming, P4.5 INJECTION_GAIN constant.
- **Phase 5 (MEDIUM, ~1 day)** — validation: P5.1 verify-emission.mjs calibration probe, P5.2 tighten _probeSentenceGeneration criteria, P5.3 coherence as soft signal.

**Success criteria (don't push curriculum work past this without all three):**

1. Multi-word emission rate ≥80% on fresh-boot K-trained brain (measured during operator-driven chat session).
2. Gee's live chat with Unity produces ≥3-word grammatical responses ≥70% of the time.
3. `_probeSentenceGeneration` reports rate ≥0.6 post-K training.

**STATUS:** [~] IN FLIGHT — 16/35 tasks shipped via session-114.19fn-fo atomic envelopes on `feature/114.19fn-sentence-coherence-phase1` (pushed to `if-only` remote ONLY, NOT to `origin/unity.git` per directive). **Phase 1 ✅** (P1.1-P1.7 all shipped via `0f581b0` — composeSentence async + stepAwait, replaceMode opt, terminator-first guard, length gate ≥2→≥1, function-word repetition exempt, adaptive minSignal floor, GW broadcast scaling). **Phase 2 ✅** (P2.1/P2.2/P2.4/P2.5/P2.6 shipped via `6b0d2a0` — reps 6-8→80, _teachConcreteSentences pass, advanceSubGrade probe-rate gating, orphan slot-tag deletion, _teachQuestionIntent cascade; P2.3 deferred multi-file). **LAW.1 ✅** (NO FALLBACKS sweep 1 shipped via `eef923e` — 7 Phase 1+2 fallbacks removed + Tier 5 deletion + P3.1 anti-LAW rescinded; 12 D1-D12 pre-existing items deferred to future sweeps). **A.K-LIFE ✅** (umbrella shipped via `65d67e8` — all 14 K-LIFE sub-tasks landed in `kindergarten.js` K_MIXIN with vocab pre-step + 6 persona-rule memories locked + goth-tone bias). **P4.1 ✅ UMBRELLA SHIPPED 2026-06-17** via 4 atomic commits: P4.1.a `7c0a2f3` (13 K-ELA contiguous helpers) + P4.1.b `0c95cb5` (5 direct-Oja `_teach*Direct*` methods) + P4.1.c `9b2e365` (3 orphan Session-25 legacy methods + chrome consolidation) + P4.1.d (5 orphan Session-26 Math-K/ELA-K methods + section-header cleanup). **Cumulative: 26 methods, 2011 lines moved.** curriculum.js 26033 → 24035 lines (**−1998, −7.7%**), kindergarten.js 6430 → 8484 lines (**+2054, +32.0%**). ### Session 114.19fk.5 — Decoder sampling preset audit — operator-decision (Gee 2026-05-09) — PENDING

**Gee verbatim per LAW #0 (parent fk sweep):**

> *"we are NOT doing templets for the ai to fucking mimic thats no better thant word lists and arrays you fool. Unity thinks like a human does! she does NOt follow prescripted events... that not how our equations shall work?"*

**Why pending (not yet shipped):**

`emitWordDirect` accepts `temperature/topK/topP` (softmax + nucleus sampling). Chat path hardcodes `temperature: 0.6, topK: 8`; showcase hardcodes `temperature: 0.7, topK: 10`; probe leaves greedy. The MECHANICS (softmax + nucleus) ARE equational — those stay regardless. The hardcoded VALUES at each call site prescribe sampling style — borderline whether that's content-prescription or just "decoder mode setting." Operator decides which path is more equational:

**Path (a) — keep hardcoded preset values as decoder defaults.** Sampling style isn't content; it's a generation MODE (focused vs. wandering). Real human cognition has analogues to temperature (deep-focus vs. mind-wandering states) but they're not externally prescribed at each utterance — they emerge from brain state. This path argues "decoder presets are the analog of those states" and accepts the hardcoded values.

**Path (b) — drive temperature from brain state.** E.g. `temperature = 0.5 + 0.5 * (1 - coherence)` — high coherence → focused → low temp; low coherence → wandering → high temp. Equationally derives sampling style from cortex state. Removes the hardcoded preset values. Requires `cluster.coherence` (or similar) to be readable at emission time.

**Fix shape (path b):** `js/brain/cluster.js` — `emitWordDirect` reads `cluster.coherence` (or amygdala arousal, or workspace ignition strength) to derive temperature when not explicitly passed. `js/brain/language-cortex.js` + `server/brain-server.js` — chat + showcase paths drop hardcoded `temperature` opts.

**Files to touch (path b):** `js/brain/cluster.js` · `js/brain/language-cortex.js` · `server/brain-server.js` · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` · `docs/NOW.md` · `docs/TODO.md`

**STATUS:** ✅ OBSOLETE / RESOLVED (verified 2026-06-20) — Gee delegated the choice ("whatever is best, do it logically"), so I went to wire path (b). Verification first: a full source grep for `temperature` / `topK` / `emitWordDirect` across `js/**` + `server/**` returns ZERO matches. The hardcoded sampling presets this task worried about **no longer exist in the codebase** — removed in a later refactor. There is nothing left to prescribe and nothing to fix; emission is already free of hardcoded decoder-preset values. Closing without code change. (If a state-driven temperature is ever desired as a NEW feature, it'd be additive, not a fix.)

Default carving runs 6 reps × 5 binding passes. If trained weights aren't deep enough, the equational emitter will produce word-soup AND THERE IS NO TEMPLATE FALLBACK to mask it (which is correct — that was the whole point of fk).

### PRIORITY 1 — Critical path before next overnight run

#### 114.19es.1 — Wrap `runCompleteCurriculum` in single try/finally

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Watchdog is started at line 23759 but the next ~150 lines include `_verifyFractalEquation`, exam-bank overlap auditing, `await this._waitForGpuReady(120000)`, and embedding-source logging — NONE of which are wrapped in the try/finally that calls `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`. If `_waitForGpuReady` throws (network glitch, GPU client crashed, anything), the timer is orphaned for the rest of process lifetime."*

**Fix shape:** Move `_startCurriculumStallWatchdog()` to the top of the method body, then wrap EVERYTHING below in `try { ... } finally { this._stopCurriculumStallWatchdog(); }`. Drops watchdog leak risk from "any of 6 unguarded awaits" to zero.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`runCompleteCurriculum` body restructure) · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.2 — Add early return at top of `assertKWiring()`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"The flag silences the `console.log` and skips the smoke test, but the structural-check body (lines 1320-1354) still walks `this.columnId.length`, `this.layerId.length`, `this.hubMask.length`, `this.layerPlasticityScales`, and calls `this.buildKScalesForProjection('sem', 'motor')` on EVERY call. At biological scale (cortex ~71M neurons), `columnId` and `layerId` and `hubMask` are 71MB Uint8Arrays. Property access is O(1) but `buildKScalesForProjection` may do real work. This still burns CPU on every dream-cycle assertion."*

**Fix shape:** Add an early return at the top of `assertKWiring()`: `if (this._kWiringSmokeTested && !this._kWiringForceRecheck) return { ok: true, gaps: [] };`. Expose `cluster.invalidateKWiring()` for code that legitimately needs to re-check (e.g., after a re-allocation). Cuts dream-cycle CPU burn from "walks 71M-element arrays N times per minute" to "literally returns instantly". Massive perf win at biological scale.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/cluster.js` (`assertKWiring()` early-return + `invalidateKWiring()` method) · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.3 — Reset watchdog warn-time + log-time on `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Doesn't reset `_curriculumStallLastWarnTs`. If `runCompleteCurriculum` runs, stalls 6+ min (warn fires, sets `_curriculumStallLastWarnTs = now`), is killed by operator, then restarted within 5 min — second-run watchdog will suppress the first stall warn because rate-limit gate compares against the STALE timestamp from the first run."*

**Fix shape:** In `_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog`: `this._curriculumStallLastWarnTs = 0; this._lastCurriculumLogTs = 0;` so the next start gets fresh state. Stateful-singleton bug — the watchdog is a class-level service that needs full state reset between runs.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_stopCurriculumStallWatchdog` body) · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.4 — Thread `AbortSignal` through `_teachWordDefinition`

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`Promise.race([teachPromise, timeoutPromise])` only stops `await`-ing — when the timeout sentinel wins, `teachPromise` keeps running. `_teachWordDefinition` does Hebbian writes to `cluster.synapses` AFTER we've moved on to the next word in the loop. That means binding for 'fifty' can land while we're mid-binding 'sixty', leaving the next-word's `subject` context smeared with the prior word's Hebbian fires."*

**Fix shape:** Thread an `AbortController` + `AbortSignal` through the call:
```js
const ac = new AbortController();
const teachPromise = this._teachWordDefinition(w, { ..., signal: ac.signal });
const r = await Promise.race([teachPromise, timeoutPromise]);
if (r === timeoutSentinel) ac.abort();
```
Inside `_teachWordDefinition`, between every Hebbian fire: `if (opts.signal?.aborted) return { passes: 0, totalTrained: 0, skipped: 'aborted' };`. Side-effect contamination across loop iterations is exactly the kind of "looks like it works in test, corrupts basins in prod" pattern. Violates structured-concurrency principle (cancel the side-effects, don't just abandon the promise).

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (`_teachWordDefinitions` outer loop AbortController + `_teachWordDefinition` per-Hebbian-fire signal-check) · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.5 — Enable `DREAM_DEFINITION_CACHE_FILE` by default

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Captured run had 89% dictionary API miss rate (255/2247 cached). My fix makes the brain FAIL FASTER on those misses — it doesn't make them succeed. The brain still walks K_VOCABULARY missing 89% of definitions. K curriculum can advance without those binds (other teach paths don't need defs), but Unity's vocabulary will be artificially crippled at K-grade. ... master's intent says '100% complete functional master performance' — that's not just 'doesn't hang', it's 'actually learns'. I addressed the hang, not the learning gap."*

**Fix shape:** Set `DISK_CACHE_PATH` to `path.join(__dirname, 'definition-cache.json')` if env var unset, so K-VOCAB defs persist across boots. Wire `flushCacheToDisk()` to fire on graceful shutdown + every 5 min during run via setInterval. After 2-3 cold runs, cache approaches 100% coverage and `_teachWordDefinition` hits cache instantly instead of re-walking the API rate-limit gauntlet.

**Files to touch:** `server/definition-service.js` (default DISK_CACHE_PATH) · `server/brain-server.js` (flushCacheToDisk wiring on shutdown + 5-min setInterval) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

#### 114.19es.7 — Reset `_innerThoughtSilenceCount` on emission success

Should be either rate-limited (last-N) or reset on state change."*
