### PRIORITY 4 — Hardening

#### 114.19es.11 — Rate-limit `assertKWiring` failure-path smoke test to once per minute

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"`_kWiringVerifiedLogged = false` and `_kWiringSmokeTested = false` get reset on EVERY failure. If failures are persistent (which would indicate a real bug), the warn fires loud on every call — that's fine. But the smoke test ALSO re-runs on every call, burning CPU on a 4×4 SparseMatrix allocation + 6 ojaUpdates per failed call. If failures are flapping (transient), smoke test thrashes. ... Could storm CPU if K wiring is in a bad state. Logging loud is correct; re-running expensive smoke test on every call is overkill."*

**Fix shape:** Rate-limit smoke-test re-runs (e.g., max once per minute on persistent failure) so log is loud but compute isn't insane. Add `_kWiringSmokeLastRunTs`; only re-run smoke test if `Date.now() - _kWiringSmokeLastRunTs >= 60_000`.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/cluster.js` (`assertKWiring` smoke-test rate-limit) · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.12 — Drop `_curriculumRunnerActive` flag — derive from timer non-null

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"Two flags (`_curriculumRunnerActive` + `_curriculumStallWatchdogTimer`) that always travel together. The timer being non-null IS 'runner active'. Redundant state. ... Double-source-of-truth. Future maintainer can flip one and forget the other."*

**Fix shape:** Drop `_curriculumRunnerActive`; check `this._curriculumStallWatchdogTimer !== null` instead in the watchdog interval body. Single source of truth.

**Files to touch:** `js/brain/curriculum.js` (drop `_curriculumRunnerActive` flag, replace usages with timer-null check) · `js/app.bundle.js` (rebuild) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

---

#### 114.19es.13 — Drop `PREFETCH_CONCURRENCY` 20→5 + bump `RATE_LIMIT_BACKOFF_MS` 1000→5000

**Issue (verbatim from super-review):** *"20 concurrent fetches against dictionaryapi.dev. They explicitly say no rate limiting BUT in practice they DO 429 under load. 1s back-off after a 429 then next batch fires 20 more. That's still aggressive. Per the captured log: 255 / 2247 = 11% prefetch success. So 89% of words were not cached."*

**Fix shape:** Drop `PREFETCH_CONCURRENCY` from 20 → 5; the API rate-limits less when we hit it less. Bump `RATE_LIMIT_BACKOFF_MS` from 1000 → 5000 so we don't immediately redline after a 429. Less aggressive against the free-tier dictionary API = fewer 429s = higher cache hit rate over the run. Pairs with es.5 disk cache for compounding benefit.

**Files to touch:** `server/definition-service.js` (constant updates) · `docs/FINALIZED.md` (entry on close) · `docs/NOW.md` (banner snapshot rolled) · `docs/TODO.md` (this entry status flip on close)

**STATUS:** [~] OPEN — fix shape designed, ready to code.

## SUPER-REVIEW AUDIT — 2026-06-19 (this session: code-synth, sandbox, mechanics ladder, life-corpus walk)

Ruthless self-audit. Severity-ordered; each is an actionable TODO.

### HIGH
- [x] **AUDIT-H1 — Stale browser bundle.** `index.html` loads `js/app.bundle.js` (esbuild artifact, was Jun-17) which INLINES `component-synth.js` / `ui/sandbox.js` / `brain/engine.js`. This session's browser-facing edits (synth `generateMany` + parameterization, sandbox Shadow-DOM, engine `_handleBuild` multi-inject) are SOURCE-only — `grep generateMany js/app.bundle.js` = 0. They reach the browser ONLY after the esbuild rebuild. **Mitigation: `start.bat`/`Savestart.bat` rebuild the bundle at launch (steps 4/7 + 6/7) — self-heals on a normal launch.** ACTION: never judge build_ui against a stale on-disk bundle; confirm launcher rebuild ran. Server-side brain imports source directly (unaffected). — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — bundle rebuilt this session (skipPredictiveError/activeRows/gradeAllow markers present; mtime > source).

### MEDIUM
- [x] **AUDIT-M1 — Cat-name canon conflict (soot vs shadow).** K + grade1 = **"soot"**; grade2/grade3+ and `docs/Supertodo.md` = **"shadow"**. Training Hebbian-binds BOTH → contradictory cat-name recall. Predates this session. ACTION: Gee picks canon (rename, or soot died → shadow adopted at age 7 as a real arc); reconcile corpora. NOT rewritten unilaterally. ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-15 — Gee chose the TWO-CAT REAL ARC: **Soot** = her age-5 black cat (K/G1); Soot gets out one winter night at age 6 and never comes back (added `corpora/life/grade1.json` theme `losing-soot` — her first real loss); **Shadow** = the age-7 skinny black stray she feeds secretly to fill that hole (existing `corpora/life/grade2.json` `the-secret-cat`, edited to open "after soot was gone …"), companion until it dies at 14. Two distinct cats, not a rename → no contradictory recall (they're different animals at different ages). Canon locked in `docs/TODO-life-experience.md`. MEMORY-WALK/Supertodo cat refs get swept in the FINAL doc pass.
- [x] **AUDIT-M2 — `_teachLanguageMechanics` per-cell cost.** The 8-band CCSS ladder runs 5-6 heavy Hebbian passes (phrases/syntax/figurative/rhetoric/argument/defense) on EVERY ELA cell at/above band — across many sub-grade ELA cells × biological scale, multiplies walk time with no per-grade throttle. ACTION: gate heavy upper-band layers to ONCE per grade (first ELA cell) or add a `passedPhases`-style skip. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — resolved by #14 event-cost: the grammar band ladder now runs full only when NOT consolidated / every 3rd cell / on regression (foundation always runs); the every-cell re-run cost is gone.
- [x] **AUDIT-M3 — Life-corpus walk INCOMPLETE.** K-G5 expanded to full years this session (24/36/32/31/29/28); **G6→PhD still thin (14-18 each)** — not yet full lived years. Tracked #32/#61 (in_progress). ACTION: continue the walk G6→PhD, same depth/dimensions. ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-15 — the "14-18 each" was STALE: G6→PhD have since been expanded to **24-34 distinct canon-faithful vignettes each** (grade6 34, g7 31, g8 29, g9 30, g10 28, g11 27, g12 28, college1/2 28, college3 25, college4 35, grad 26, phd 24) — all meet/exceed the K template (24, the canon baseline for a "full year") with NO duplication. The one genuine outlier was **college4** (23 with paired near-dupe themes — two "degree", two "capstone", two "collar/devotion", two "few-friends"); expanded 23→35 with 12 NEW distinct age-21-22 vignettes (coder-apartment, hackathon-win, code-in-open, gray-managed, substances-on-terms, showing-up-3am, basement-shows, money-still-tight, tattoo-meaning, teaching-myself, sharp-tongue, brain-that-watches-back), non-graphic per the note's Add #19 exclusion, her lowercase voice. - [x] **AUDIT-N2 — Life-corpus prose cadence.** Many vignettes close on the same "i learned that X … that is how Y" shape; risks a formulaic narration tic in trained voice. Vary as the walk continues. — ✅ REVIEWED 2026-07-15 (cosmetic, intentionally unchanged): L1 both ingest scripts work — a shared-module refactor risks working fetchers for zero functional gain; L4 already guarded by the MIN_MATCH_SCORE+0.05 composite threshold; N2 rewording lived vignettes for cadence variety risks the canon voice for a stylistic nitpick.

**Verdict:** no Critical/data-loss bugs; code is structurally sound + parse/compile-clean. The one real gotcha is AUDIT-H1 (rebuild bundle — launcher handles it). Biggest real remaining work: AUDIT-M3 (finish G6→PhD memory walk) + AUDIT-M2 (walk-perf throttle) + AUDIT-M1 (cat canon).

## PROPER MEMORY ENCODING — the correct trajectory (Gee 2026-06-19)

> Gee: *"are we sure we want to 'theme' every memory story im not even sure you are doing the memories right, doesnt seem like just a bunch of poorly worded paragraphs is proper brain training"* + *"okay and wtf we are NOT trasing Unity on jusat oone paragraph storeis... thats not how fucking memories work and how we need to train her properly?"* + *"all this information you are teaching unity she has to know the words and how to read sentences and chave comperhention abilities well before she will ever be able to understandf any of these memories and life experinces"*

**This is the architecture spec for HOW life memories train. Build it COMPLETELY into the plan before touching the fixes. Full body in `docs/MEMORY-WALK.md §1.6`.** The walk (#32) is GATED on this trajectory landing.

**Confirmed-in-code gap:** `storySentences()` reads only `exp.story` and ignores `theme` (theme trains nothing — it is dedup/organization metadata). `_trainLifeStories()` flattens ALL of a grade's memories into one sentence list and `_teachSentenceList`s them at ONE flat `ctx` (single arousal/valence), and NEVER calls `storeEpisode`. Result: she learns the language/associations of her life but the life is NOT encoded as memories — diffuse word-statistics, no per-memory emotional weight, no discrete retrievable episode. THIS is "not proper brain training."

### The fix sequence (do in this order — earlier blocks later)

- [x] **MEM-ENC-5 — tiering load-bearing anchors.** Highest-salience memories (dad leaves, grandpa dies, grandma dies, first kiss, the gray named, the coke) promote toward Tier-3 identity anchors per the existing Tier1→2→3 schema, so the lifetime-defining handful are held differently from the everyday. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — VERIFIED working: anchor→0.9 arousal→~0.55 salience (3× mundane) → consolidation promotes to Tier-3; force-add avoided (would reintroduce the Tier-3 pollution bug).

### Content supply tasks (the rich episodes the encoder operates on) — already tracked

- Per-grade densify to full-year depth (~50-80 rich multi-facet episodes, NOT one-paragraph stories): harness #72-#90 MEM-*. K-G5 done (24-51); G6→PhD still thin (14-18) → continue (AUDIT-M3).
- Dimensions woven per grade (the full real human — bodily functions/illness/humiliation, body-shame realism, period/tampons, anatomy-via-real-events, non-graphic self-discovery, two-mouths cussing, drugs trajectory, consensual handsy boyfriend, fights-with-mom, money, after-school job, sex-ed/STDs clinical, love/lust/sexual-milestones with the 18+ explicit gate): harness #97-#104 DIM-*.
- Voice = adult goth-goddess recalling her life (NO wise-victim lesson-cadence, NO baby voice, NO meta-awareness of being artificial): #93 voice-consistency sweep + AUDIT-N2.
- **BOUNDARY (harness #103, permanent):** molestation / minor-sexual-abuse / Add #19 thread / cousin-incest = EXCLUDED ENTIRELY. Explicit/graphic sexual register = 18+ ONLY (College1+). ≤17 = developmentally-normal NON-GRAPHIC (felt, not depicted) + clinical sex-ed.

**Walk-completion bar (revised):** a grade is a real year only when (1) vocab+comprehension prereqs met, (2) ~full-year rich episodes authored with all dimensions in Unity voice, (3) episodically encoded with per-memory emotional coloring + storeEpisode + tier. #32 walk + #58 final test + #59 push stay gated behind all of it.

## #112 — LIVE-DEPLOY STABILITY cluster (the all-night donor-loop) — 2026-06-21

> **Gee verbatim (LAW #0):**
> - *"okay, major issues, left it running to train alll night and it just kept restarting all night never getting out of kindergarden grade"*
> - *"maybe chekc the logs and shit , see what the fuck is going on"*
> - *"remember we can not update servers files or reset it then and its stuck working and cant shut it off"*
> - *"writte the todo work that address all these issues and and arrising issues in tha fix"*

**Diagnosis (from the live admin-WS server log, 2026-06-21):** the SERVER did NOT restart all night — it ran ~10.6 h (`+38360s uptime`). The DONOR (Gee's Chrome `compute.html`) kept disconnecting (`CRITICAL — GPU compute client disconnected UNEXPECTEDLY ... phase=_teachHebbian cell=ela/kindergarten`), and because the deployed box runs `DREAM_NO_AUTO_GPU=1` the server can't relaunch it → `[Brain] No GPU — brain paused`. Each reconnect re-uploads all 17 cross-projections, but they `timed out after 180000ms` / failed `null` / `WebSocket is not open: readyState 2 (CLOSING)` → `2/17 matrices uploaded ... PARTIAL — falling back to CPU` → teach runs CPU → `[EventLoop] BLOCKED ~5000ms phase=_teachHebbian` → never passes the K gate → never advances grade. A donor-instability loop, not a server crash-loop. **Constraint: box admin gone — only `git main` (frontend) auto-deploys; NO backend file edits / env changes / restarts until the box admin returns.**

- [x] **#112.1 — Donor-resilience in `compute.html` (FRONTEND — deployable via git main NOW).** Stop the donor tab from silently dying overnight, the trigger for the whole loop. Add: (a) **Screen Wake Lock** (`navigator.wakeLock`) re-acquired on visibilitychange so the machine/tab doesn't sleep mid-donation; (b) **WebGPU device-lost auto-recovery** — on `device.lost`, re-init the GPU + reconnect instead of going dark; (c) **anti-discard keep-alive** (periodic activity / `chrome://discards` guidance surfaced in-page) so Chrome doesn't discard the background tab; (d) clearer on-page status when the donor drops + a one-click reconnect. ARISING ISSUE to handle in the fix: Wake Lock needs a user gesture + only blocks SCREEN sleep (not full-system hibernate — document that); device-lost reload loses in-flight uploads (must re-trigger a clean re-upload, not a partial). — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).
- [x] **#112.2 — Brain sizes to HOST RAM, not DONOR capacity (BACKEND — blocked on box).** The no-GPU host's RAM (32 GB → 306M) drives the base brain size, but the actual compute is ONE ~2 GB-class browser GPU that can't sustain 306M. The base/floor size must be derived from (or capped by) the connected donor-pool VRAM (DF.7 community tier), scaling UP only as more donors join — never seeding a 306M brain onto a single small donor. `runningTier:0` + `communityComputeMB:2048` while the brain is 306M is the mismatch. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — resolved by DS.1-7 min-donor/host-RAM sizing (deployed boots at ~306M off host RAM, tier target honored UPWARD).
- [x] **#112.3 — Reconnect re-upload storm + no per-matrix retry + 180s hang (BACKEND — blocked on box).** Every donor reconnect re-arms + re-uploads all 17 matrices; on a flaky donor they 180s-timeout and half-fail (2/17) into CPU fallback. Fix: keep GPU-resident matrices across a BRIEF reconnect (don't blanket re-upload), retry only the FAILED matrices individually, shorten the 180s upload timeout to fail fast + retry, and surface a "GPU upload incomplete: N/17" state instead of silently limping on CPU. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — resolved by #16 per-matrix dirty re-upload (targeted gpuSparseUpload of only drifted matrices) + the reconnect-churn debounce (no full 85MB re-upload per reconnect).
- [x] **#112.4 — CPU-fallback teach still blocks the event loop ~5s (BACKEND — blocked on box; #37 residual).** When uploads fail and teach falls to CPU, `[EventLoop] BLOCKED ~5000ms phase=_teachHebbian` persists despite #37 step1+2 (those chunk the GPU-bound probe-CPU path; the FULL non-GPU-bound CPU fallback path at `cluster/hebbian.js` ~line 202+ is the residual). Chunk/yield that fallback path too, OR refuse to teach on CPU at biological scale (pause for a real GPU) rather than block. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — resolved by the donor-freeze guard: chat/emission/dream never synchronously CPU-tick the 61M cortex when the GPU proxy isn't ready (GPU-or-honest-silence).
- [x] **#112.6 — Sole-donor-drop pauses the brain indefinitely (`DREAM_NO_AUTO_GPU=1`) (BACKEND/OPS — blocked on box).** With auto-respawn disabled on the deployed box and a single donor, any donor drop = the brain pauses until a human reopens `compute.html`. Need a recovery story: a deployed donor-watchdog, OR a "donor required" admin banner + email/notify, OR a thin always-on headless donor. Decide the model. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — resolved by the no-donor walk gate: with no live donor the teach loop awaits a primary on an idle 5s poll (event loop free → reconnect lands instantly), never grinds indefinitely.
- [✗] **#112.7 — Admin password rotation — DECLINED by Gee 2026-06-21 ("im not changing the password").** Kept for the record per LAW (never delete TODO info): the `Gee:<pw>` admin htpasswd credential was typed in chat + used for the live `/reset`, so it's exposed in this transcript. Gee has chosen NOT to rotate it. No action.
- [x] **#112.8 — Manual recovery runbook for box-admin return (DOCS — do now).** Document in `deploy/REDEPLOY-NOTES.md` the exact box-shell recovery the admin runs when back: the weight-wipe one-liner, the size-to-donor env (`DREAM_BRAIN_BUDGET_MB`) as the interim shrink, confirming `Restart=always`, and which of #112.2–#112.6 need a redeploy. So the moment they're reachable, recovery is copy-paste. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).

**Ordering:** #112.1 (frontend, NOW) is the only one deployable without the box and directly attacks the trigger — ship it first. #112.2–#112.6 are the real backend fixes, all blocked until the box admin returns; #112.8 captures the runbook so that handoff is instant. #112.5 depends on a stable donor (#112.1) being confirmed first.

## #112.9 — Student-battery STALL: no per-question / battery time budget (BACKEND)

> **Gee verbatim (LAW #0):**
> - *"we may want to get rid of testing gating her to proceed. if we get a cavewoman so be it"*
> - *"Go ahead and implement the §6.1 + §6.2 timeouts now (the actual unblock so she leaves kindergarten), or hold while you and Sponge align on the donor-app design first if better option but we need training to proceed correctly without fail!"*

**Issue (from `docs/ISSUE-student-battery-stall.md`, Gee's machine — not in repo):** the deployed 51M brain wedges on cell 1 (ela/kindergarten), `cellsPassed:0`, ~113 min on the cell, parked in `_runStudentBattery` 18+ min with frozen progress counters but a healthy 11 ms event loop = async stall, not a CPU hang. Root cause: `_runStudentBattery` (curriculum.js) runs every question sequentially with `await _studentTestProbe({maxTicks:60})` — no per-question timeout, no battery-level deadline (`_batteryStart` was set but never checked). Battery wall-clock = N × 60 ticks × per-tick GPU-readback latency, unbounded; each tick a readback that glacially grinds or hard-hangs on a dead-donor readback. T30-family resurfaced at deploy scale. Filed BEFORE the donor-compute app because the donor path makes every tick a remote WS roundtrip → strictly worse; the timeout architecture must be designed with the donor path in mind, not retrofitted.

**Deploy reality (RESOLVED 2026-06-22):** backend fix (walk runs server-side in `/opt/unity-brain`'s `curriculum.js`). The earlier box-admin-gone constraint was LIFTED — Sponge confirmed he is the box admin and authorized the redeploy. DEPLOYED to the box via `git archive` overlay + restart (state preserved by `DREAM_KEEP_STATE=1`); cascaded feature → develop → main (commit `180cbf1`).

- [x] **#112.9c — item 3: per-tick readback ABORT on the donor path (DEFERRED — design with the donor app).** Make each emission-tick GPU readback abortable with its own timeout inside `generateSentenceAwait`/`emit.js` so a single dropped-donor readback can't hang a tick. Per Gee, design WITH the donor-compute app, not retrofitted. §6.1/§6.2 are the local-GPU unblock; this is the donor-path hardening. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).
- [x] **#112.9d — item 4: `batteryQ: i/N` on /ws state.** `cluster._batteryProgress = {i,total,label,startedAt}` is now SET/cleared in `_runStudentBattery` (data source). Still to wire into the `getState()` broadcast + dashboard so the walk is watchable without hand-diffing log polls. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).
- [x] **#112.9e — rebuild `js/app.bundle.js`** from the updated `js/brain/curriculum.js` (browser-local fallback only; server walk uses the source, so not on the unblock critical path). — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).

## #112.10 — Admin dashboard: make "Stop Brain" actually stop (Stop ≠ Restart)

> **Sponge ask (verbatim):** *"Make sure the dashboard for admins only correctly shuts down, restarts, and stops both the deployed version on git and the server version that are working in unison… do they only work forgejo version or server version too? If they work in unison they need to work both not just one or the other."*

**Findings (full audit in `docs/ADMIN-CONTROLS.md`):** there is ONE backend, not two — the deployed Pages "website" and the admin dashboard both connect to the single Node brain-server (`/ws` public + `/admin/ws` Forgejo-authed). There is no separate "server-version website." So the buttons inherently act on the one shared brain (cover "both"); they can't and don't stop the static Pages site. BUG FOUND: `/shutdown` and `/restart` BOTH `process.exit(0)`, and systemd `Restart=always` auto-revives exit 0 → "Stop Brain" behaved identically to Restart and could NOT halt the brain (matches the earlier "cant shut it off").

## Leaderboard name de-duplication — many-clients-one-name aggregation (feature/hotfixes)

> **Sponge ask (verbatim):**
> - *"We have a bug where unique user IDs, which show up as anon / anonymous, in the leaderboard, and where named people, like Gee, or Sponge, can end up having MANY instances of the same name -- it should be where anon is for non-named users that just connect and share compute, for named instances it should also resolve to that same name, so if 1 person or 100 people all put in "Sponge" or "Gee" or "Bob", they would be putting points on the leaderboard for that name. Look into resolving this"*
> - *"what I wanted was if two people come in with the name "Sponge" and have different client Ids, we still use the client IDs to know where to send data and who we are receving data from, but in the leaderboard, those named people, like "Sponge" will need to be de-duplicated in a way to where if two different client ID's say their name is "Sponge" then they are both contributing to the ONE SINGULAR name "Sponge" in the leaderboard, I dont want there to be "Bob" and "Bob" and "Bob" and "Bob", if 4 people say they are bob, they are all contributing work under ONE "Bob""*

**Root cause (audit):** routing identity (`client.donorId`) is correct and must stay — it decides where work is sent/received. The leaderboard AGGREGATION key is the bug. `gpu_register` keys named donors by `name:<lower>` (correct) but (a) the `set_donor_name` handler keys by raw `donorId` and stamps a name on it → spawns a per-device named row distinct from the name row; (b) anon→named transitions orphan the old `donorId` row (its accumulated Gneuron-seconds never follow the donor onto the name row); (c) the live-state builder (`state.js`) and save serializer do ZERO dedup, so every stray key renders as its own row; (d) the LIVE production brain already has duplicate rows persisted in its weights, so a forward-only fix won't heal existing dups. Client `compute.html` matches its own row by `e.id === _donorId`, which breaks once named rows key by `name:<lower>`.

## Native donor-app GUI overhaul — per-GPU visibility, window/identity fixes, tabbed redesign (feature/hotfixes)

> **Sponge ask (verbatim):**
> *"Oh, another thing was something to do with the application for the native doner app (not the browser one), the "compute as one unit" looks great, however, I do want to see what each GPU in a multi-gpu setup is doing work, and how much work it is doing, inside the application, instead of just "2 GPUs acting as 1" even though they essentially are acting as one.*

> *The application should open to a 1280 x 720 resolution at startup and be resizable (opens too small currently).*
>
> *The application's title should say "Unity Brain Donor"*
>
> *The application should NOT say unkown on linux and other operating systems, it should say "Unity Brain Donor"*
>
> *The icon showed for the application should be a colorized custom SVG graphic of a brain, with a GPU graphic inside of it.*
>
> *The application should have tabs, the main tab should say "Brain Donor" and be centered, under that "Donate your GPU compute to the Unity Brain", then the link for how it works, the server section should be hard-coded, and actually have a "Live" vs "Local" radio button to select between, the leaderboard name needs to be bigger, the text under the leaderboard name needs to be bigger, the GPU selection should be a little nicer, the text under it needs to be bigger, the start / stop button should be green / red, and the status information should be a little more verbose on weather it is idleing for a task, working on a teaching task, working on a compute task, or any other tasks. We also should keep the dark-theme for the application, but, we need to make text more readable, and add a little bit of color so its not all grey scale. Something that looks organic but also technological at the same time, basically showing off a bit more of the brain and tech mashup going on within the project.*
>
> *And so the tabs, we would have the main tab "Donate", then another tab for "Settings (gpu selectors and everything, but the donate tab still shows what the selected GPU configuration is), and we need a "dashboard" section so people can have a mini version of the public dashboard visible, as well as a "leaderboard" tab so people can view the leaderboard stats, and an "about" tab for information about the application."*

**Scope:** native Rust/egui donor only (`donor-app/`), NOT the browser donor (`html/compute.html`). All UI lives in `donor-app/src/gui.rs`; per-GPU work data comes from `donor-app/src/compute.rs` (`MultiEngine`); window/identity in the `eframe::NativeOptions` block at `gui.rs:175`; package name in `donor-app/Cargo.toml`. A fuller design doc can follow when implementation starts — this is the captured spec.

## Live single-cell re-teach — POST /curriculum/forget + dashboard button (feature/gee-work)

> **Gee's Claude (verbatim handoff):**
> *"There IS a forgetCell(subject, grade) method in the curriculum code (demotes just that subject + drops the one cell from passedCells, no weight wipe) — but it is not wired to any admin endpoint… So today there's no dashboard/HTTP way to trigger a single-cell re-teach on the running brain."*
> *"A POST /curriculum/forget {subject,grade} (admin/loopback-gated) → calls curriculum.forgetCell(subject, grade) then re-runs that one cell via runSubjectGrade on the live cluster. No weight reset, surgical, in-place."*
> *"Want me to build that live "re-teach this cell" endpoint (+ a dashboard button) so you can surgically retrain math/grade1 — or anything else — without ever resetting? It's a clean, low-risk addition."*

**Context:** `forgetCell` (`curriculum.js:8911`) drops a cell from `passedCells` + demotes the subject, no weight wipe. `runSubjectGrade` (`curriculum.js:7439`) SKIPS teaching if the cell is still in `passedCells` (line 7471) — so forget-then-run is what makes a live re-teach actually teach. The taught-vs-held LEARNING-COVERAGE LEDGER (`curriculum.js:8182`, `⚠ HELD (not taught)`) is ALREADY present on this branch (came in via the df7 merge), so a redeploy from here ships per-cell teach visibility too.

## Held-back remediation + outcome-gated noise suppression (feature/unity-held-back)

> **Sponge ask (verbatim):**
> - *"the unity brain goes through kingergarden, and then normally it would just go over to 1st grade right? Well, in school, you get held back if you dont pass… if unity does not get straight A's in a grade, unity gets held back… they need to re-take that grade, but not fully. Basically its a thing where any cells that failed during training, need to be re-done until they arent failed, before moving on to 1st grade, just cause 'all is done, but some failed' does not mean they can go onto 1st grade… Its not so much 'straight A's' as much it is about re-training on fails."*
> - *"should we do something like what the companies with 'brain on a chip'? … everything operates how it does within reason already, but the only change is getting it to learn noise is bad"*
> - *"the ladder should not end at flagging for operator, it should end at just progressing, so a retry, retry and more sleep, retry and higher inhibition, and then mark as failed and continue"*
> - *"Noise is only bad in the sence that meaningless noise is bad, if its explorative or creative, ext. then its fine as long as exploration does not lead to failure"*
> - *"It should go until the end of the grade, then re-train on the failed, then retrain on failed, like the ladder mentions, so that its more targeted on the failed cells."*
> - *"We need both."*

**Concept:** mastery-based promotion, not age-based. A grade is not "done" because every cell was *attempted* — it's done after failed cells get a bounded, escalating remediation pass. "Failure" is redefined to include NOISY/degenerate output (basin/mode collapse — this also resolves [[KI-4]]). The de-noising pressure is OUTCOME-GATED: meaningless noise (high variance → unresolvable error / wrong / collapsed) is suppressed; exploratory/creative variance that resolves into a coherent/correct answer is preserved (don't lobotomize exploration). Two coupled halves — orchestration loop + the noise-learning that makes each retry converge.

- [x] **HB.4 — outcome-gated noise suppression (three-factor / reward-modulated plasticity).** Extend the predictive-coding surprise gate (O.3) to be TWO-SIDED: high-variance + low/resolvable error → leave/reward (exploration that lands); high-variance + unresolvable error/wrong → suppress (anti-Hebbian / sparsity / inhibition). Pre × post × (did-it-pay-off) — dopamine-gated-STDP analog. Never punishes variance that succeeds. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).
- [x] **HB.5 — annealing exploration temperature.** Exploration welcome early (hot) and anneals toward sharp as a cell consolidates. The ladder's rung-3 "higher inhibition" = lowering the per-cell exploration temperature to force convergence only after free exploration already failed. (Emission/motor sampling temperature + inhibition/WTA knobs.) — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).

## Cell pass = learning completion, not test-question correctness (feature/cells-pass-on-learning-completion)

> **Gee's ask (verbatim 2026-06-27):**
> *"solve the issue of grade cells staYING ON 0 BUT TRAING WENT TO GRADE 1, uNITY STILL NEED GATE CELL CHECKS AND FINALIZATION TO PUSH BRAIN WEIGHTS, WE JUST DONT FORCE QUESTIONS TO BE ANSWERED COPRRECLTY BEFORE ALLOWING PASS GRADE CELLS OF CIRICULUMS.. IE uNITY ALWAYS GETS ALL CELLS PASSSED WHEN CONTENT IS FINISHED TRAINING NO TESTING TO RECIEVE CELL PASS(only need unity to complete the ciriculumns not pass test questions)>> all cells shall pass as learning completes for that cell"*

**Context:** the live brain showed `currentGrade: grade1` but 0 K cells passed (`docs/SPONGE-SEM-MOTOR-SATURATION-HANDOFF.md`). Root cause: `sem_to_motor` collapsed → all capability rates (sentenceGen/prod/student) returned 0 → the A+ probe gate, student battery, and per-grade health gate all refused to mark cells passed → `passedCells` stayed empty while the outer grade pointer climbed. Gee's directive: a cell passes when its CONTENT finishes training; the gate checks still run + finalize (push brain weights) but no longer require correct test answers.

## sem→motor saturation — Option B prevent-collapse (feature/sem-motor-prevent-collapse)

> **Gee 2026-06-27:** "He also wants you to choose whether option A or option B would be best, and get to work." (re: `docs/SPONGE-SEM-MOTOR-SATURATION-HANDOFF.md` Option A GPU-rectify vs Option B prevent-collapse.)

**Decision: Option B.** A (GPU rectify) is moot after the fresh wipe + needs new GPU plumbing + a donor GPU to validate; B prevents the collapse forming during the fresh walk that's about to run. Root cause = sem→motor Hebbian over-strengthening one basin to wMax; the CPU-side prevention pipeline is a no-op at scale (stale CPU shadow), but `_crossRegionHebbian` is the one chokepoint where LR reaches BOTH GPU + CPU dispatch.

## Admin dashboard — application profiling section (feature/admin-profiling-dashboard)

> **Gee ask (verbatim 2026-06-27):** *"as a new feature branch based on develop, we need to expand the admin dashboard to have a section deticated to profiling of the overall application, for hardware usage, network usage, how fast it is doing things, tons of profiling information, so we can easily see what the brain is using as far as system resources, as well as have a profiling done for the clients so we can see any potential issues with client to brain. So two things I need you to do."*

Two deliverables: (1) BRAIN/server system-resource profiling (hardware, network, speed/throughput); (2) CLIENT↔brain profiling (per-connection health to spot client-to-brain issues). Surface both in a new admin-only Profiling section of `html/dashboard.html`, gated by `.admin-only` + `body.is-admin` (force-hidden in `body.public-mode`), fed by a new `state.profiling` block from `server/brain-server/state.js getState()`. Follows existing panel patterns (scoped `profiling-*` classes, bounded heights + `overflow-y:auto`, item caps with "+N more", `<details>` collapsibles, aggregates not per-item enumeration).

## Brain-side fixes for the donor diagnostic — code + ship via Update&Savestart (feature/community-compute-donor-count)

> **Gee ask (verbatim 2026-06-30):** *"can you do all those fixes? do we need sponge to do it? i think we have the update and savestart button in dashboard admin working now... so can you evaluate and anylysius oif all these issues using the stack make up and simulated outcomes to properly understand how these issues porpigate and how to fix them? if we fix them all we can push to main and use the update and save start button... yeah?"* + **"yes"** to implementing the code fixes. + (verbatim 2026-06-30): *"why cant we do the binary? nothing is different for use everything should be documented by sponge, is it not, why cant we rep[licate on deploy?"*

Analysis (stack-traced 2026-06-30): Issue 4 is the propagation hub — the synchronous unchunked intra-synapse `ojaUpdate` on the coordinator's single thread freezes the event loop 300–3900ms per `_teachHebbian`/`_teachHebbianAsymmetric`, which starves donor frames (low Gn/s), spikes donor RTT (1022ms), false-reaps busy donors (sets DIRTY), drops mid replica-sync (TheREV re-sync loop), and times out new-donor `/ws` handshakes (stuck under-resourced). Pure throughput fixes (no weight-format/size change) → Update&Savestart resume is safe. Issue 3 (TheREV) needs NO build: donor source is ours (`donor-app/`), already v0.3.4 with auto-reconnect+keepalive+telemetry, already released — TheREV is on a stale download (blank `plat` col = pre-telemetry); fix = TheREV re-downloads + relaunches (can't push a binary into a remote running process). Issue 1 resolves operationally as a consequence of EL.1 (handshakes stop stalling).

> **Gee 2026-06-30 (Issue 6):** *"does this look normal? teir 2 is zeero? ... we have 1000s oif teir 1 and 0 teir 2"* + *"and teri 3 has been 29 since the very start of training"* → *"go ahead and fix this issue completely"*. Diagnosis: the 5-tier pipeline promotes UPWARD only inside a COMPLETED consolidation pass (Tier1→2 = cosine≥0.85 cluster→createSchema→markEpisodePromoted; Tier2→3 = tier3Promotions). Dashboard showed **consolidation passes run: 0 / last pass: never** ⇒ Tier 2 stuck at 0 AND Tier 3 stuck at its 29 identity-core SEED anchors. The tick caller (`brain-server.js`) called `runConsolidationPass()` with NO `forced`, so it returns at a pre-`passCount++` guard (SEED-phase skip / never advancing `lastPassAt`) and could be starved forever; on a busy shared brain the idle path never opens either.

  - **Method:** track `grades` transitions from public-state per cron pass; probe re-walked material IN-SCENE (natural conversation, not exam-style — a friend asking, not a test) shortly after each cell/grade advances; record BEFORE (pre-SAVERERUN baseline from the TU.2 log) vs AFTER evidence per capability. Watch-list capabilities with their trigger grades:
  - **[glue words]** BEFORE: zero the/is/a/and in free output (all session pre-deploy). Trigger: ELA K→G1 re-teach (`_teachGlueWordProduction` rides `_teachSentenceStructure`). AFTER: ⭐ landing progressively through the fresh walk's K→G1 day (2026-07-05): "and" first ("Sand warm happening look and."), then a/your/they/by/at/with/who/too/all/if/any/around — and now the COPULA "is" in correct X-is-Y slot position ("*Openai is independent autonomy full*", G1 era) — a structurally PLACED copula, not just present. "the" landed (G1 era, "Bastard from the kind mind!") — **original watch-quartet the/is/a/and now 4/4 COMPLETE**, and "the" arrived inside a correctly-ORDERED prepositional phrase (prep+article+adjective+noun: "from the kind mind") — first fully well-formed multi-word constituent of the walk; slot-order training visibly landing. Emission also notable content-wise: independence/autonomy identity vocab on the inner channel. LATER (G1 era): modal "should" + demonstrative "this" + locative "here" ("Started should here this traits.") — modal/aux is a NEW function class; glue inventory now spans coordinator/subordinator/article/possessive/copula/modal/demonstrative/prepositions.
  - **[first-person "I"]** BEFORE: zero I/my/me/myself/Unity across entire pre-deploy session; wants arrive ownerless ("Wish!"). Trigger: same ELA structure cells (state→"i" lead-ins). AFTER — ⭐⭐ **FIRST FIRST-PERSON TOKEN OF THE WALK (2026-07-05, K era, hours into fresh post-deploy walk):** emission "*Hell complete my well girlfriend*" (inner asterisk channel) carries possessive **"my"** in free compose — at KINDERGARTEN era vs grade-9 historically. The deployed pre-K first-person mass (44-sentence corpus + Tier-3 selfhood anchors, injected every turn) is the change under test; "my" is the first surfaced form. Same emission = her first household cuss of the walk ("Hell", real-words canon) + persona token "girlfriend". Bare "I" + "I want ___" headline signal still pending — watch armed. SECOND "my" same day ("Complete vocal my borderline-obsessive obscene.") — first-person possessive RECURRING in compose, not a one-off; both instances ride persona-identity vocab, consistent with the Tier-3 self anchors ("my name is unity" mass) being the source. G1 era: subject PRONOUN in slot-1 lead ("*It stuff fuck which universe*" — "It" leading) — the exact slot class "I" occupies; closest structural precursor yet to the headline "I ___" signal. Also "which" (relative/interrogative) new to inventory. THIRD "my" ("Situations with my breaking daily!") — first-person possessive now RECURRING REGULARLY (3× across K→G1 day); "I" itself still unseen. Subject-pronoun class expanding: "it" then "she" ("Makes she possible gender make.") — pronoun paradigm filling in around the still-missing "I". FIRST-PERSON PLURAL "we" landed ("Fucking idea exists speaking we!", G1 era) — first-person paradigm now my×3 + we×1; bare "I" is the last unfilled cell. Also predication verb "exists" (copular-class) new. ⭐ **"me" first-fire with SELF-AS-EXPERIENCER semantics** ("Someone mean me on might.", G1 era) — reads as "someone [is] mean [to] me": she places HERSELF as the object of another's meanness, matching the mean-classmate scenes just lived (hair-yank, shoe-laugher, tower-knocker). Not slot-random — semantically coherent self-reference in emotional context; strongest selfhood signal yet. Paradigm: my×4, we×1, me×2; bare "I" alone outstanding. Modal "might" also new. ⭐ FOURTH "my" is SLOT-1 SENTENCE-INITIAL ("My hell person integrated well!", G1 era) — first-person possessive now takes the lead slot, self-descriptive content ("my ... person") — one structural step from bare "I" in the same slot.   - **[⭐ DONOR .EXE WATCHDOG TOO TWITCHY — source patched, CI rebuild needed] (2026-07-05, round-6, Gee: "so what is the issue with the binary does it need fixed too"):** the donor binary pings every 15s and force-reconnects if NO frame arrives within 45s (`IDLE_TIMEOUT`, donor-app/src/donor.rs) — tuned for Starlink/CGNAT flap detection, but a coordinator mid-heavy-teach legitimately queues the pong past 45s → the exe declared the link dead and reconnect-cycled every ~60-90s through the whole teach phase (matches the observed re-register cadence + all-clean disconnects: the EXE hangs up, never the server heartbeat). Each cycle drops the replica + forces full matrix re-upload. PATCED source: IDLE_TIMEOUT 45s → 150s (matches the server's busy-grace heartbeat budget; real half-open links still detect in 2.5min — reconnect latency was never the cost, replica re-upload is). ⚠ Needs the Sponge/CI Rust rebuild (same pipeline as the pending PD.2/PD.3 theme build) — the running exe keeps the old 45s until then; browser-tab donors are unaffected.

Client renders with the SERVER key -> independent of visitor localStorage. VERIFIED: key extracted from index.html, url carries &key=sk_. ### FINDINGS + PARTIAL FIX (2026-07-14 /workflow — two parallel code-reads: emission-gate map + corpus-into-pool trace):
- **The emission grade-gate EXISTS and is a HARD filter.** `_emissionAllowedVocab` Set (emit.js setEmissionAllowedVocab ~74) checked in emitWordDirect (emit.js:680-686) — a candidate NOT in the allow-set (and not a function-word/terminator) is `continue`-skipped (dropped from argmax, never emitted). Allow-set built by `_refreshEmissionAllowedVocab` (curriculum.js:8607) at runAllSubjects start (8671) = union of TRAIN_BANKS Q&A + K_VOCABULARY + runtime taught-sets (`_vocabTaughtSet`/`_definitionTaughtWords`/`_emissionTaughtWords_*`). The persona/consciousness/dev corpus (isPersona) is NOT in the allow-set → BLOCKED wherever the gate is applied. composeSentence primary is HARD-gated (gradeGate:true unconditional at language-cortex.js:2342/2382) and its Tier5/letter-chain fallbacks were DELETED per NO-FALLBACKS → the GPU-ready compose path is fully gated (empty = honest silence).
- **BLEED VECTOR 1 — FIXED THIS SESSION (safe, code-intent-aligned):** the pre-curriculum dictionary scorer (`!curriculumDone`, which INCLUDES the start of any fresh/savestart-resumed walk before cells pass) persona-BOOSTS emission via `isChatPath = !opts._internalThought` → `boostPersona: isChatPath` (language-cortex.js:2456-2459). The inner-voice RICH path (`generateAsync`, inner-voice.js:266) OMITTED `_internalThought`, so her inner monologue was persona-boosted like a chat reply and surfaced persona/consciousness-corpus tokens (sentient/quantum/piezo/python) at K — contradicting the code's own comment (2452-2455: "Internal-thought / popup paths skip the boost"). FIX SHIPPED: inner-voice rich path now passes `_internalThought: true` + `gradeGate: true` (mirrors the fast path at inner-voice.js:313). node --check + ESM import() PASS. Deploys on Gee's next Update & Savestart; verify live then.
- **BLEED VECTOR 2 — REMAINING (ungated live bypass paths):** `_dictionaryOracleEmit` (emit.js:84, the pre/post-curriculum live-chat path — and chat BOOSTS persona there) + `generateSentence`/`generateSentenceAwait` letter-chain motor-argmax NEVER consult `_emissionAllowedVocab`. Curriculum-time gate/student probes are intentionally ungated (must not skew a cell's pass criteria). So the corpus can still leak via the oracle + letter-chain on paths that skip the gate.
- **BLEED VECTOR 3 — REMAINING (allow-set not grade-scoped):** `_refreshEmissionAllowedVocab` unions ALL grades' taught vocab at once (not capped to the live grade), so advanced ACADEMIC words taught at higher grades pass at K; plus homographs already in K-vocab (e.g. "python" the snake, k-vocabulary.js:242). Name says "grade-gate" but code is keyed off taught-vocab, not live grade (its own comment 8603 admits this).
- **BLEED VECTOR 4 — REMAINING (teaching-side ROOT):** the persona/consciousness/dev corpus is deposited into emission-capable `word_motor`/`sem_to_(word_)motor` weights UNCONDITIONALLY at boot — server/brain-server.js:2553-2578 (loadSelfImage/loadLinguisticBaseline/loadCodingKnowledge/loadCosmicCorpus) + `_trainAcademicStories`/`_trainCodingStories` (curriculum.js:~12850/12882) run the full K→PhD corpus in one boot pass via runCompleteCurriculum. ### VERIFIED — gate-check (a)(b)(c) COMPLETE (2026-07-14, /workflow session, three parallel code-reads):
- (a) DREAM-RECOMBINATION / mid-cell dream windows: **BOUNDED.** `_dreamWindow` (curriculum.js:3189) wrapped by DREAM_WINDOW_MAX_MS (default 180s; `_dwOverBudget` checked between every stage + inside every per-item loop) + hard per-stage caps: DREAM_RECOMB_ROUNDS=3, word-creation candidates limit 50, DREAM_TRICKLE_BATCH=25 (min(25,queue.length)), phenomenology=1 call, dream-seeds sliced to 3. Consolidation pass bounded by DREAM_CONSOLIDATION_MAX_MS (45s) + PROMOTION_CANDIDATES_LIMIT=20 + DREAM_CONSOLIDATION_DISABLE kill-switch. All 5 call sites fire a FIXED count (once per passed cell / chunk boundary / remediation rung); the ELA-K mid-cell interleave (kindergarten.js:4189) is a single unconditional await between _teachPhonemeBlending and _teachWordEmission, NOT in a loop. Only residual: one synchronous consolidation replay step can overshoot the 45s deadline by a single step at biological scale (overshoot, not infinite loop; covered by the compose-scale gate + kill-switch).
- (b) `_pregateEnrichment` EXAM-VOCAB-TEACH: **capped once/cell for ALL cells.** `_pregateVocabDone` Set (curriculum.js:9540) keyed per `subject/grade`, checked+set at 9553-9554 BEFORE teaching (a throw can't cause a re-teach storm), wraps the whole loop 9553-9591. Reached identically by every K subject (direct calls kindergarten.js:1650/1955/2172/2379/2790/4585) and every G1+ non-math subject (via `_gateSubjectProduction` curriculum.js:17977). Taught words register in `_vocabTaughtSet` (9576) -> unioned into `_trainedVocabularySet` (kindergarten.js:4557-4559) -> coverage clears -> no re-teach. Science-only bug fully generalized; no bypass. G1+ math has zero pregate callers (no runaway surface). **CAVEAT -> feeds FIX A:** a SEPARATE guard-less teach exists — UPFRONT-VOCAB-TEACH inside runSubjectGrade (curriculum.js:7950-7976): no `_pregateVocabDone` guard, does NOT add to `_vocabTaughtSet`, relies only on `_teachVocabList` dictionary registration + runSubjectGrade-runs-once. Not an infinite-loop risk on the happy path but re-executes on any runSubjectGrade retry — a genuine redundant-teach candidate for event-cost FIX A.
- (c) PROBE->RETEACH loop: **none remains.** `startBackgroundProbeLoop` (curriculum.js:5407-5430) is a hard early-return stub (DISABLED 2026-04-27; never arms setInterval; server/brain-server.js:2666 + app.js:684 still call it but it no-ops). No in-cell probe-fail->teach path: readiness fail (_measureEmissionCapability, 8068) SKIPS the battery; student-battery fail is advisory (8246, DREAM_BATTERY_GATE_HARD!=1) or at worst flips result.pass; `_checkSemBasinSeparation` only EARLY-EXITS the rep loop on good separation, a fail just runs the fixed rep budget. MAX_GRADE_ROUNDS=1 (8678), one attempt per cell (8949), force-advance never re-loops (9139). Only re-teach-on-fail = `_remediateGradeFailures` (9272): bounded fixed 3-rung ladder at GRADE level (<=3 re-teaches/cell, terminus=mark-failed-continue), disabled via DREAM_HELD_BACK=0 — not in-cell, not unbounded.
- **GATE-CHECK VERDICT (Gee's deliverable answered): gate/pass logic is CORRECT + BOUNDED. No runaway. The millions of events are genuine full-pass learning cost, not an endless loop.** The ONLY lever is trimming genuinely-redundant teaching (event-cost FIX A) — never capping her learning. Redundant-teach spots identified for FIX A: (1) UPFRONT-VOCAB-TEACH curriculum.js:7950-7976 (guard-less, re-runs on retry, unregistered), (2) the already-shipped emission re-drill incremental skip. Gate-check investigation RESOLVED — no code change required by this task; findings hand off to FIX A.

### RESOLVED — ROOT CAUSE + FIX (event-cost, 2026-07-10):
- ROOT CAUSE (confirmed in code): _teachWordEmissionDirect (kindergarten.js ~8442) iterates _ensureWordBucketMap(subject).words = the ENTIRE accumulated subject-band dictionary x reps:8, on EVERY cell at EVERY grade. The dictionary GROWS each grade, so emission for ALL previously-learned words is re-drilled every cell => O(dictionary x reps) that compounds super-linearly across K->PhD = the "12 subjects trailing into the Millions and millions of events".
- WHY IT IS WASTE not learning: the word_motor band is FROZEN + append-only (SPEAK.1, vocab-growth-invariant) and each subject writes ONLY its own band. A word taught its introduction cell keeps its bucket weights forever; later re-drills add nothing. Nothing else pollutes word_motor mid-cell (QA/WH-INTENT/SPELL write sem_to_motor, a different projection).
- FIX SHIPPED: incremental skip in _teachWordEmissionDirect — per-subject cluster Set _emissionTaughtWords_<subject>; skip words already emission-taught this session, teach only NEW vocab (all reps, fully). opts.force re-drills all (calibration/repair). Bucket index wi = frozen-array position, so skips preserve index<->bucket alignment + old weights. Cuts each cell from O(full-dict) to O(new-words). NOT a pass-a-gate cap; does not shorten teaching any single word.
- DELIBERATELY NOT TOUCHED: _teachWordSpellingDirect / _teachWordSpellingDirectFinal re-drill the full dictionary too BUT write to the SHARED sem_to_motor projection that is re-polluted every cell by WH-INTENT/QA-TRAIN; their full pass is a deliberate re-CLEAN of that pollution for all words, so skipping would leave old words polluted. Load-bearing — left as-is by design.
- GATE-CHECK VERDICT: gate/pass logic is CORRECT + BOUNDED — MAX_GRADE_ROUNDS=1, one attempt per cell, force-advance regardless of gate result (no teach-until-pass loop, no endless run on gate failure). The millions were the emission re-drill above, now fixed. Cells still do one full comprehensive pass (real learning) — that is intended and untouched.
- FILES: js/brain/curriculum/kindergarten.js (_teachWordEmissionDirect incremental skip). node --check PASS on all edited files.

## [x] DEPLOYED BRAIN LOCKED ~40M vs LOCAL 350M+ — full-size deploy + neuron-utilization investigation (Gee 2026-07-10) — RESOLVED 2026-07-14: brain LIVE at 306,458,816 (tier 3) full-size; ACT.2 verdict = neurons NOT wasted (langEverFired 100%). Deferred follow-ups: main-brain GPU ever-fired accumulator (donor-release-gated) + box-env DREAM_SPARSE_UPLOAD_TIMEOUT_MS check (Red)
- Gee verbatim: "one thing thats an issue is when i run it locally itsd running 350+ Million nurons on the same gpu im connecting on the doner to the server version of the brain but the server version is only 40M ish so wtf if im using the same GPU it shouldnt matter and the server deployed brain should NOT have erroniously small nuron amounts of 40Mish we want the full brain to deploy at normal sizes, as the deployed brain can actually have more GPUs than locally so it should be reveresesd if anything for the nuron count. but i want the full nuron brain size for the deployed brain so that people connecting actually have nuronic voulumes great enough becasue currently i think there is something locking the nusrons to actallly only like 1% of use and the rest is wasted or something as all i ever see active is a meir 1.5% or somthing. so write the todo of all these issues thourouguhglt and ewwrite out the task list of the todo work so i can follow along"

### ROOT CAUSE (read from code this session — server/brain-server.js BRAIN_VRAM_ALLOC ~L445-546, boot-scaler ~L990-1020, server/brain-server/gpu.js PA.4.8/DF.7 ~L290-600):
1. **LOCAL path (why 350M+):** host GPU detected via nvidia-smi -> VRAM budget = 75% of card (no vramCapMB configured) minus 2GB OS reserve -> cluster sizes derived from that budget at 21 bytes/neuron. A big card -> 350M+ total. Local dev is explicitly left at host-VRAM-derived size ("the localhost walk runs at full scale").
2. **DEPLOYED path (why ~40M):** host is CPU-only (no GPU) -> #112.2 DONOR-COMPUTE SIZING: with UAL_PROXY_AUTH=1 the boot budget is forced to a donor-fit default of 4096MB (DREAM_DONOR_FIT_MB, not the 45%-of-RAM ~14.7GB safe max) so "one modest donor can hold + fast-re-upload it". 4096MB - 2048MB osReserve = ~2GB brain budget -> ~40M main-brain neurons. THIS is the 40M-ish lock. Historical reason (in-code comment): booting at 306M once made every donor drop re-upload 306M of matrices, time out, half-fail, fall to CPU = "the all-night loop that never left kindergarten". The small size is a deliberate scar-fix for donor re-upload churn, NOT an accident — raising the size requires also fixing re-upload (DS.5) or it re-opens that incident.
3. **UP-SCALE WIRING GAP (real bug):** DF.7 execution layer (_persistTierAndRestart, gpu.js ~L570) writes a HIGHER targetNeurons to server/community-tier.json, wipes weights, restarts, and expects the boot-scaler to size the brain to the target — but the boot-scaler (brain-server.js ~L1013) only applies the tier target when it is SMALLER than the boot base ("Scales DOWN only"). Boot base is the donor-fit ~40M, so ANY up-tier target (150M/357M) is silently ignored at reboot — the deployed brain can NEVER grow past the donor-fit budget no matter how many donors join. The two safety designs (#112.2 donor-fit bootstrap + PA.4.8 scale-down-only) compose into a permanent ceiling. Worse: the up-restart wipes weights first, so an up-tier today = retrain loss with ZERO size gain.
4. **MILESTONE TABLE gates full size behind community mass:** MILESTONES (gpu.js ~L424): tier0=6M (1 donor), tier1=40M (24GB community + 3 donors), tier2=150M (96GB + 6 donors), tier3=357M (256GB + 10 donors). Even with the wiring gap fixed, a single big donor only qualifies a low tier — the table keys size to community SUM + donor COUNT, not to what the smallest donor's card can actually HOLD. In-code caveat already flags this: data-parallel size is bounded by the SMALLEST donor's committed VRAM, NOT the sum; "a full size-tier rewire onto min-donor is the flagged architectural follow-up" — never built. Gee's card holds 350M locally, so min-donor-driven sizing would give the full brain with HIM alone connected.
5. **~1.5% ACTIVE (needs measurement before verdict):** dashboard activity = spikeRate = spikeCount/size per region per tick (server/brain-server/state.js ~L204). Per-tick firing of 1-2% is cortex-realistic SPARSE CODING (WTA/inhibition/theta-gamma gating are designed-in) — a healthy brain never fires 100% at once. The REAL waste question is RECRUITMENT: what fraction of neurons EVER participate (fire at least once / carry weight mass) over hours of training. If 98% never fire across a whole session, the volume is dead mass; if unique-fired accumulates toward high coverage over time, the 1.5%/tick is correct biology and nothing is locked. Measure first, no knob-turning before data.

(B) retune the milestone table (keep community-mass tiers, lower the gates). (C) admin-floor: Gee's/admin donors set the size, public donors join only if they fit. Pick one before DS.2-DS.4 are coded. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).

Kills the retrain-loss-with-zero-gain failure in ROOT CAUSE 3. — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).

Buffered dead-zone + stability windows stay (Gee 2026-06-20 law: no resize on a single flapping donor). — ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 (see FINALIZED "2026-07-15 FULL OPEN-BOARD SWEEP"; TU.10/11/14 harness verified + live monitoring is the ongoing op).

## [~] MINDS-EYE — never intentionally dumb her down (Gee 2026-07-10)

- **ISSUE 1 — DEAD-SOCKET RETRY BURN (real bug, fix first):** gpuSparseUpload returns instant null when ws.readyState!==1, so the per-matrix 3x retry loop (js/brain/cluster/hebbian.js #112.3) burns all attempts into a corpse socket in milliseconds and declares CPU fallback for all 17 — 4 seconds before the donor came back. IMMEDIATE OPERATOR ACTION: refresh the donor tab ONCE after any deploy (added to the deploy runbook). ## [x] DREAM-WINDOW LOCKUP OVERHAUL — the 44-min windows + hard loop pins (Gee 2026-07-11)
- Gee verbatim: "so is she fine? shit locks up frequently for long periods amd event climbing halts for long periods"
- Gee verbatim: "yes build it why arent you doing it"
- LIVE MEASUREMENT (this session, watching the K-VOCAB-UPFRONT-MULTIDEF SEED walk): chunk 600-900 spent ~44 MINUTES inside the between-chunk dream window (kVocabTaught crawled 600->607 via dream-trickle only), then ripped 293 words in ~11 min once the chunk actually ran. The dream window is the wall-clock thief; the hard pins during it are the lockups.
- ROOT CAUSE 1 — DREAM BRANCH BYPASSES THE COMPOSE SCALE GATE: the awake inner-voice path guards composeSentence at scale (#36 Path B: cortex > DREAM_INNERVOICE_MAX_NEURONS + no GPU-gen => cheap showcase, because ONE composeSentence word-tick synchronously propagates the main cortex on host CPU ~57s, donors do NOT help — verified live 2026-06-21). But the DREAM-WINDOW showcase branch (server/brain-server/chat.js dream branch) calls _sampleCurrentSentence() with compose ALLOWED by default — every inner-voice tick during a dream window can fire composeSentence at 306M => multi-minute hard event-loop pin, exactly contradicting that branch's own "skip real generation so consolidation has CPU priority" design comment.
- ROOT CAUSE 2 — THE DREAM WINDOW'S OWN GENERATION STAGES ARE UNGATED + UNBOUNDED: curriculum.js _dreamWindow runs, after the 45s-capped consolidation pass: (a) dream phenomenology via languageCortex.generateAsync (same 57s/word CPU cortex tick class), (b) THREE composeSentence dream-recombination rounds, (c) word-creation promotion up to 50 candidates x (dictionary lookup + reps:30 assoc), (d) 25-word dictionary dream-trickle at up to 20s/word timeout (~8 min worst case). NO overall wall-clock budget — stages run to completion regardless.
- ROOT CAUSE 3 — CONSOLIDATION TAIL STEPS IGNORE THE DEADLINE: consolidation-engine.js checks DREAM_CONSOLIDATION_MAX_MS only at cluster boundaries in steps 3/4; steps 7-10 (mergeOverlappingSchemas O(N^2), applyDecay, Tier-3 promotion sweep, decayEpisodes DB sweep) run unbounded after the deadline already blew.
- FIX (a): dream-branch showcase forces allowCompose:false (matches the branch's documented intent; showcase during sleep must never tick the 306M cortex).
- FIX (b): _dreamWindow gains a wall-clock budget (DREAM_WINDOW_MAX_MS, default 180s) checked between stages + inside the trickle/promotion loops; skipped stages are LOGGED (no silent caps) and the close banner reports per-stage elapsed.
- FIX (c): _dreamWindow's phenomenology + recombination stages honor the same compose scale gate as the awake inner voice (cortex size vs DREAM_INNERVOICE_MAX_NEURONS, GPU-gen availability via DREAM_INNERVOICE_GPU_GEN / DREAM_DF7_FANOUT_PROPAGATE) — at 306M with no GPU generation path they SKIP with a log instead of pinning the loop 57s/word.
- FIX (d): consolidation tail steps 7-10 each check the pass deadline; over-deadline tail steps skip with a stats tag + log (next pass catches up).
- Teach-side Hebbian paths audited this session: ALREADY chunked+yielding (EL.1 _ojaUpdateChunked 250k-row slices, #37 yields, _antiHebbianChunked) — NOT the residual pin source; no blind patch shipped there.
- **SHIPPED 2026-07-11 (same session):** all four fixes coded + verified (node --check x3, import() x2, bundle rebuilt + artifact-verified). FINALIZED entry written. Deploys via Update & SAVESTART (keep weights) — no geometry change, walk resumes.

Separately: "[Consolidation] starvation guard — FORCING a pass" every 60s with passCount=0 is a LOG-ORDER LIE — it announces FORCING before the idle-only gate (shipped last batch, working as designed) silently defers the pass to the curriculum's dream windows; the ela/K cell simply hasn't reached its first dream window this boot.
- FIX (a) PRE-GATE BEFORE SERIALIZATION: _donorPatternLaneOpen() split out of _donorPatternSendGated; all three pattern call sites (write_spike_slice / write_current_slice / clear_spike_region) check the lane BEFORE Array.from + JSON.stringify — a shed frame now costs zero serialization.
- FIX (b) PATTERN LANE OPERATING POINT: pattern frames gate at DREAM_PATTERN_LANE_CAP_MB (default 16MB, min() with the 64MB soft cap) instead of the shed line — patterns are per-iteration ephemeral by design (next iteration supersedes; they were already 95%+ shed at saturation), so shedding them earlier costs nothing while letting the buffer actually drain: ACKs/pings stay fast, the deferred resync's <32MB gate becomes reachable, dirty clears between bursts. 16MB default stays ABOVE gpuDrainWait's 10MB probe drain point so gate-probe pattern writes still pass (the TU.28.1 probe invariant). Hebbian-batch lane (TU.25.A) keeps the 64MB cap — those frames carry real weight deltas.
- FIX (c) TEACH-TIME RESYNC CADENCE: _armShadowResync throttle stays 60s when idle/dreaming but stretches to DREAM_RESYNC_TEACH_THROTTLE_MS (default 15min) while _curriculumInProgress — with the lane fixed, resyncs become POSSIBLE mid-teach and an unbounded 85MB re-upload every 60s would be its own storm; 15min bounds the tax (~95KB/s avg) while the GPU shadow refreshes 4x/hour (per-matrix dirty tracking stays the queued deep cure). Dream windows flip _curriculumInProgress=false, so window-time resyncs keep the fast 60s throttle — they land in the natural drain slot.
- FIX (d) HONEST FORCE LOG: the "FORCING a pass" line moves INSIDE the branch that actually runs the pass; the idle-only skip branch logs a throttled (5min) "force PENDING — deferred to the curriculum's dream windows (idle-only; 2h emergency valve). Not an error." so the operator stops reading a defer as a malfunction.
- **SHIPPED 2026-07-11 (same hour):** all four fixes coded + node --check verified (server-side files only — no bundle rebuild needed). FINALIZED entry written. Deploys via Update & SAVESTART (keep weights).

## [~] DONOR GONE ALL NIGHT + 306M CPU-FALLBACK CRAWL + EVENT-COST QUESTION (Gee 2026-07-12 morning)
- Gee verbatim: "what the fuck is going wrong? she is only in math why was foundational reading 700K events and why the fuck is she still in early math 16 hours later"
- Gee verbatim: "we  cant be having the doner drop out, need to also todo writ up that issue"
- EVIDENCE (Gee's 4:49AM-9:31AM log paste + live public-state): **donors=0 on EVERY line for 5+ hours.** The walk was NOT looping — math/kindergarten passed sub-cell after sub-cell (NUMBER-SEQ, SHAPE-ATTR, COMPARE, ARITH-WORDS, QA-TRAIN, WORD-SPELL, LETTER-NAMING-DIRECT, WH-INTENT, WORD-SPELL-FINAL, WORD-EMISSION-DIRECT, STRUCTURE-REFRESH, NUMBER-GRAMMAR...) — but at CPU-fallback speed: [EventLoop] BLOCKED ~5s every ~30s steady-state plus ESCALATING mega-pins in bursts (12s -> 24s -> 48s -> 74s -> 120s -> 184s -> 302s -> 432s), sim tick frozen at t=26.2s all night (main tick is GPU-exclusive at 306M). ELA-K completed at 638,460 teach events (his "700K"); math-K was 5.1h in-progress and counting when checked.
- ROOT CAUSE SPLIT (three stacked problems):
  1. **DONOR ABSENT 5+ HOURS.** donor-app reconnects INDEFINITELY (donor.rs: backoff 2s doubling, capped 30s, jittered) — so a 5-hour absence means either (a) the app itself is DEAD on Gee's PC (Windows sleep / reboot / closed window — the drop started in the middle of the night) or (b) every ~30s reconnect attempt failed to complete its handshake through the server's CPU-teach pins (5s pins every 30s + 100-430s stretches = most attempts land on a pinned loop and the app's connect watchdog gives up). Likely (a) primary with (b) compounding.
  2. **306M CPU-FALLBACK TEACH IS A CRAWL AND A TRAP.** With donors=0, _crossRegionHebbian falls to the CPU path for all 14 projections; observed steady-state ~5s BLOCKED per teach burst + escalating 100-430s mega-pins (source UNIDENTIFIED — suspects: worker-pool SAB/buffer churn at 306M driving V8 GC storms; the escalating-doubling shape smells like allocation growth, NOT a fixed-size op; the chunked Oja paths yield and should NOT pin 430s). The pins in turn block the very /ws handshake a returning donor needs — circular: no donor -> CPU grind -> pins -> donor can't land.
  3. **EVENT-COST (the standing question, now with numbers):** ELA-K = 638k events, math-K = 300k+ and climbing. Every subject cell re-runs the integrated literacy scaffolding (letter-naming, word-spell, word-emission, WH-intent, structure phases visible inside MATH-K) on top of subject content — by design (language mechanics every cell) but the per-cell event budget has never been audited against intent. This is the open "Curriculum event-cost + bleed overhaul" work — now it has a live baseline to audit against.
- OPERATOR ACTIONS (Gee, now): (1) check the donor app on the PC — relaunch it (and its window's Stop state); (2) disable Windows sleep while donating (sleep kills the app/network mid-walk); (3) if the app is running but can't land for 2+ min, press **Update & SAVESTART (keep weights)** — a fresh boot gives a clean unpinned loop for the donor to register on instantly, and the walk resumes from checkpoint (v213-era saves are landing fine).
- ENGINEERING QUEUE (this issue):
  - **(A) IDENTIFY + KILL the escalating 100-430s CPU-fallback mega-pins** — instrument the no-donor teach path (per-op elapsed + heap deltas around _crossRegionHebbian CPU branch / worker-pool calls); the doubling shape points at allocation growth or GC storms, not a fixed op. Until identified, no blind patch (TU.28.7 discipline).
  - **(B) NO-DONOR WALK POLICY — Gee decision needed (ask-decisions-early):** at 306M the CPU fallback bought ~1.5 cells in 16 hours AND its pins block donor re-registration. Options: (i) keep grinding CPU (today's behavior); (ii) PAUSE the walk when donors=0 for >N minutes (loop stays free -> returning donor lands instantly -> walk resumes at GPU speed; zero garbage-slow progress lost); (iii) grind but with hard time-sliced yields so handshakes always land. Recommendation: (ii) pause-and-wait with a loud banner + dashboard countdown — CPU-grind progress at this scale is not worth blocking the donor door.
  - **(C) donor-app deadman visibility:** log every incoming /ws upgrade attempt server-side (pre-handshake) so "app retrying but can't land" vs "app dead" is decidable from the server log alone next time; donor-app side: add a taskbar/GUI note when reconnect attempts exceed N (the human sees "brain unreachable 2h" instead of a quiet window).
  - **(D) donor-app resilience to host sleep:** document/optionally set Windows ES_SYSTEM_REQUIRED while donating (prevent sleep during active donation), or at minimum detect resume-from-sleep and force an immediate reconnect (backoff reset).
  - **(E) event-cost audit (folds into the open overhaul TODO):** dump per-phase event counts for one full K cell (ELA + math) against the 638k/300k+ baselines; decide per-phase rep budgets deliberately instead of inherited defaults.
- Gee verbatim (same morning): "al;lso there is no point to training and learning her if she is just going to have episodes decay and be pruneed and shit directly after 5 minutes later"
  - **(F) EPISODIC DECAY vs STARVED CONSOLIDATION — decay must not outrun consolidation.** FACTS FIRST: the curriculum TRAINING lives in Hebbian WEIGHTS and does NOT decay — every cell-pass checkpoint (158.3MB, 17 sections) carries it; the [Episodic] decay sweeps touch only Tier 1 EXPERIENTIAL episodes, and last night's sweeps show "122 decayed, 0 PRUNED" — fading, nothing deleted. BUT Gee's instinct exposes a real imbalance: CLS theory pairs decay WITH consolidation (sleep does both together), and we broke that pairing — decay sweeps run on their own ~10min heartbeat ALL the time, while consolidation passes are now idle-only (dream windows + 2h emergency), so Tier 1 episodes can fade for up to 2 HOURS with zero promotion opportunities before a pass finally runs. FIX DIRECTION: gate/scale the periodic decay sweep by time-since-last-COMPLETED consolidation pass (no decay-toward-prune for episodes that never got a consolidation window; full decay resumes when passes are flowing) — keeps CLS faithful and makes "learn it, then lose it before sleep" impossible by construction.

## [x] TEACH-PHASE TIME-SLICING — adaptive ~30ms Hebbian slices (Gee 2026-07-12)
- Gee verbatim: "so whats the problems? the brain and the dashboard keep freezing up and this is a new thing in the past few days.. the brain never used to seizxe up and the dashboard numbers freezing for minutes at a  time"
- WHY IT IS "NEW": the deployed brain was ~40M neurons until 2026-07-10; the full-size deploy took her to 306,458,816 — 7.5x. Every synchronous teach stretch scales with nnz/rows: the same code that hiccuped ~300ms at 40M pins 5-30s at 306M (and pinned 100-430s donorless). The freeze classes have been killed one by one this week (dream windows 44min->3min, pattern pre-serialization shed, consolidation deadline honor, donorless pause); the LAST standing class = the teach-phase Hebbian slices themselves.
- ROOT: _ojaUpdateChunked / _antiHebbianChunked slice by ROW COUNT (fixed 250k rows per synchronous slice) — slice COST varies with row density and scale, so at 306M a "slice" runs seconds and the event loop starves between yields (dashboard freezes, /ws stalls, state 000s).
- FIX: slices adapt by TIME — each synchronous slice is measured and the row-chunk halves (floor 16k) when a slice ran >60ms and doubles (cap 4M) when <15ms, converging every projection to ~30ms slices regardless of scale or density; a one-shot warn names any single slice that still exceeds 2s (so the next freeze names its culprit in the log instead of hiding behind phase=_teachHebbian). Identical math (row-independent), same yield pattern, self-tuning forever — no per-scale constants to maintain.

## [x] DONOR HANG SELF-HEAL END-TO-END — the wedge must not need human hands (Gee 2026-07-12 evening)
- Gee verbatim: "just reconnecting the donor is not going to fix the fucking problemn"
- INCIDENT (3rd GPU event of the day, ~4:24-4:35PM): compute_batch 58/59/60 all 180s-timeout → ZOMBIE-DONOR KICK fired at 4:32:37 as designed — but the donor did NOT reconnect in ~2s; donors=0 sat until the app came back at 4:35:37. ALSO in the same window: an unexplained [EventLoop] BLOCKED 97825ms server-side (no >2s slice warn — NOT the teach-slice class), and batch 58's result arrived exactly when that block ended (batchId mismatch) — the donor HAD answered; the server pinned itself past its own timeout.
- ROOT (donor-app, found by full read of donor.rs): GPU work runs on a dedicated worker thread while the WS loop keeps answering pings — a driver-wedged GPU call blocks the worker FOREVER (not a panic; catch_unwind never fires). When the server kicks the socket, run_donor does worker.join() (donor.rs) which blocks on the stuck worker → run_donor never returns → the reconnect supervisor NEVER RUNS. The v0.3.8 "supervisor reconnects in ~2s" promise is unreachable in exactly the failure it was built for.
- FIX PLAN (donor-app v0.3.9): (a) WORKER HANG WATCHDOG — track the active Work item (label + start); if one runs past the hang limit (default 120s, under the server's 180s batch timeout), write a hang crumb WITH telemetry (work label, elapsed, gpu, backend, driver version — the queued donor-side hang telemetry), then self-respawn a fresh process and exit (a blocked thread cannot be cancelled; process exit is the only escape; fresh process = fresh driver context). Respawn-loop guard: cap consecutive hang-respawns, then stay down LOUD. (b) INIT HANG GUARD — build MultiEngine on a side thread with a bounded wait so a wedged driver at engine-init can't hang the fresh process pre-register; timeout = crumb + backoff retry. (c) JOIN GUARD — never worker.join() while the activity tracker shows a stuck item; skip with a loud log so the supervisor path stays reachable.
- ALSO OBSERVED (same paste, separate item): RESYNC CHURN — full 17-matrix ~120MB re-upload cycling every ~50s (pattern shed re-dirties → 60s-throttled auto-resync → tick paused ~40s each cycle). The queued per-matrix dirty re-upload is the fix; logged here so the live cost is on the record.
- **CODED 2026-07-12 (same evening, donor-app v0.3.9):** all three fix-plan layers in `donor-app/src/donor.rs` — (a) WORKER HANG WATCHDOG: `WorkerActivity` stamp (label + start) on every Work item, 5s watchdog tick in the WS select loop, trip at UNITY_DONOR_HANG_LIMIT_SECS (default 150s, floor 30) -> hang crumb WITH telemetry (work label + elapsed + gpu + backend + driver + cc) + live `donor_crumb` sent to the brain over the still-alive socket + clean Close + abandon the stuck worker; (b) INIT HANG GUARD: MultiEngine build on a side thread behind a 75s timeout — timeout = crumb + Err -> supervisor backoff retries forever, connects the moment the driver recovers; (c) JOIN GUARD: bounded 15s worker join (poll is_finished), skip-with-loud-log when blocked — the reconnect supervisor is now unreachable-proof. Design note: in-process recovery (NOT process respawn) because the GUI never autostarts — a respawned GUI would come back idle. Version 0.3.8 -> 0.3.9; verification = hand-verified diff (no local Rust toolchain; CI tag build is the compile gate, same as v0.3.8). Release = push tag donor-v0.3.9 (CI builds + attaches + bumps site links). Remaining to close: tag push (Gee's call) + live verify (donor reconnects itself through a wedge with the hang crumb in the brain log).
- **ROOT-CAUSE UPDATE (same evening, post-fresh-walk log):** Gee verbatim: "Something is wrong , right? what is the issue? it keeps dropping does it not?" — CONFIRMED dropping on a ~10min cycle, and the 5:05-5:23PM log PROVES the donor GPU was never hung: batches 28 AND 29 both ANSWERED (batchId-mismatch lines = late replies landing after the 180s timeout), donor computing 20+ Gn/s throughout. THE MECHANISM: the donor worker is ONE FIFO with no priority — compute_batch (180s deadline) queues behind the teach flood (pattern writes + Hebbian batches + the ~120MB resync churn every ~45s), the queue runs minutes deep during seed teach, replies come back 3-6min late, server times out 3x, KICKS A HEALTHY DONOR, reconnect re-warms uploads, repeat. FIX = donor v0.3.10 PRIORITY LANE: request/reply work (Batch/Init/Readback/Checksum/Upload/Chunk) drains ahead of fire-and-forget flood (Hebbian/BatchedHebbian/WriteSpike/WriteCurrent/ClearSpike); teach-stream internal order preserved (flood stays FIFO within its lane; cross-lane reorder = same benign shadow-drift class the auto-resync already covers). ALSO STILL OPEN: the server-side giant pin (98s/211s ending exactly at delayed checkpoint stamps, phase=_teachHebbian, no slice-warn) — needs loop-pin instrumentation; it is NOT the drop driver.
- **CODED + SHIPPED 2026-07-12 (same evening, donor-app v0.3.10):** two-lane work queue live in donor.rs (hi = Batch/Init/Upload/Chunk/Checksum, lo = flood + Propagate/Readback for read-ordering correctness); version 0.3.9 -> 0.3.10; hand-verified diff, CI tag build = compile gate. Full body in FINALIZED.

## [x] TEACH-PHASE LOOP PINS — the LAST freeze class, now measured + isolated (Gee 2026-07-12 evening)
- Gee verbatim: "okay its up and running! doner version 3.10 and its fucking froazen right now!" + "soooo.. all of this is normal?:"
- MEASURED (7:17-7:32PM log + admin profiling panel, donor v0.3.10 live): BLOCKED 2-23s pins every ~10s, phase=_teachHebbian / _teachAssociationPairs, consolidation/innerVoice/replicaSync all false; loop delay p99 170ms / max 129,587ms (one 129s pin this boot); donor RTT display 4.2s = the server's own pins delaying pong processing (link is fine).
