## [~] WMB REGRESSION — pre-cell seed ~100x slower after langCortexSize 349K→1.5M (Gee 2026-07-14)

- [x] **K-CELL 100× ROOT (Gee 2026-07-15, live log: sustained BLOCKED on _teachWordIntegrated).** The predictive-error carry helped but the REAL cell pin was per-word full-1.5M spike clears: _teachWordIntegrated + _teachVocabList/_teachSentenceList/_teachSequenceCycles/concept-teach zeroed the WHOLE cluster before each per-letter/per-word tile-write (~48 full clears/word in _teachWordIntegrated alone). ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — _writeTiledPattern only SETS active dims so the clear is needed but only over written regions; added _clearRegionSpans + _clearCortexRegionSpans scoped-clear helpers, replaced all 9 per-item full-clears (letter+phon+motor / sem+motor / +free for concept-teach). O(size)→O(region), bit-identical. Deploy = Update & SAVESTART. See FINALIZED 2026-07-15.

- [x] **WMB REGRESSION — CARRY FIX TO ALL GRADES (Gee 2026-07-15: "did we not carry over those fixes for all grades?").** Seed went fast but K CELLS ran ~100× slower — FIX 1/2 were gated on relationTagId===23 (def seed only); non-def cell pairs (rel 8/9/13/34) still fired the full per-pair _teachPredictiveError (~45M-nnz propagate at 1.5M). ✅ DONE 2026-07-15 — skipPredictiveError now defaults ON for ALL association binds (opts.keepPredictiveError to restore); scoped _clearSpikes now universal. SAFE: binding rides cross-projection Hebbian; intra still trained by _teachHebbian; HB.4 surprise (_lastPredictionError) set independently (cluster.js:3574). Deploy = Update & SAVESTART (keep weights, no geometry change). See FINALIZED 2026-07-15.
- Gee verbatim: *"is it normal that training is now 100x slower in precell setup so far????? investigate and analysis and todo of issues"*.
- NOT normal: langCortexSize grew 349K→1.5M = 4.3x more neurons; teach cost should be ~4-5x, NOT 100x. Something in the K-VOCAB-UPFRONT-MULTIDEF SEED path scales SUPER-LINEARLY with cortex size and the grow exposed it.
- SUSPECTS to trace: (a) a full-`cluster.size` alloc per-word/per-def (NOT pooled) → at 1.5M = 12MB/alloc × thousands = GC catastrophe; (b) the CPU word_motor projections (`sem_to_word_motor`/`word_motor_to_sem` showed `:CPU` in the _crossRegionHebbian diag — the other 14 are GPU-fast) running UNSLICED synchronous ojaUpdate per word at 4.3x scale; (c) an O(size^2) op (dense-ish projection nnz, or a sync loop nested over size); (d) worker-pool SAB / scratch-buffer threshold thrash at the bigger size; (e) intra re-upload now 360MB (was 85MB) if the seed triggers frequent resyncs. INVESTIGATE before any change (TU.28.7 no-blind-patch).

### ANALYSIS (code-read 2026-07-14) — NOT a new bug, the grow EXPOSED a long-standing "full-cortex cost for a sem-LOCAL op" inefficiency:
- No O(size^2), no unpooled alloc, no dense matrix (intra + cross are fanout-sparse; all big buffers pooled). The seed is a STACK of O(cluster.size) full-cortex sweeps fired per def-token pair, when only ~few-thousand sem neurons are active. At 349K tolerable; at 1.5M each sweep is 4.3x bigger AND spills L3→DRAM (per-element cost rises) → compounds to ~100x. This IS the standing "event-cost overhaul" theme, now urgent.
- **FIX 1 (biggest lever) — skip `_teachPredictiveError` for the definition whitelist.** curriculum.js:13551 fires it per-pair inside `_teachAssociationPairs`; it runs the full-nnz intra `propagate` (~1.5B mul-adds/pair, the single heaviest teach op) but definitions bind sem↔fineType — the recurrent-intra prediction correction adds ~nothing to a def bind. Gate it off when the whitelist is the def whitelist (or sem_to_motor not in the target set).
- **FIX 2 — scope `_clearSpikes` to touched region spans.** curriculum.js:10420-10423 zeroes all cluster.size ×2/pair; the seed only writes sem (+ fineType tag). Clear only those spans (or undo written indices) → O(regionSize) not O(1.5M).
- **FIX 3 (bigger) — iterate ACTIVE spike indices, not all rows.** sparse-matrix.js:776/827 intra Oja/anti scan all `rows` even though real work is ~5K sem rows; + drop the per-def K-scaled secondary full-cortex Oja (curriculum.js:12207-12228, redundant on top of the cross-projection bind). Convert to active-set iteration.
- ALL THREE convert O(cluster.size) → O(active-sem-region) → the seed runs fast at ANY cortex size. Teach-path changes → verify by reading + a fresh walk. Recommend FIX 1 + FIX 2 first (high lever, low risk); FIX 3 is the deeper active-set refactor.
